   240	def test_openai_provider_bad_request_not_retried():
   241	    from app.core.config import settings
   242	
   243	    settings.OPENAI_API_KEY = "openai-key"
   244	    settings.OPENAI_MODEL = "openai-model"
   245	    provider = OpenAIVisionProvider.__new__(OpenAIVisionProvider)
   246	    provider.provider_name = "openai"
   247	    provider.analysis_type = AnalysisType.OPENAI_VLM
   248	    provider.model_name = "openai-model"
   249	
   250	    class DummyBadRequestError(Exception):
   251	        pass
   252	
   253	    class DummyResponses:
   254	        def __init__(self):
   255	            self.calls = 0
   256	
   257	        async def create(self, **kwargs):
   258	            self.calls += 1
   259	            raise DummyBadRequestError()
   260	
   261	    provider.client = SimpleNamespace(responses=DummyResponses())
   262	    provider._map_error = lambda exc: OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 요청 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="VISION_REQUEST_INVALID", status_code=400, detail="openai bad request")
   263	    with pytest.raises(OpenAIVisionError) as exc_info:
   264	        asyncio.run(
   265	            provider.analyze(
   266	                before_image=b"before",
   267	                before_mime_type="image/jpeg",
   268	                after_image=b"after",
   269	                after_mime_type="image/png",
   270	                menu_items=[VisionMenuInput(meal_menu_item_id=1, menu_id=10, menu_name="제육볶음")],
   271	            )
   272	        )
   273	    assert exc_info.value.code == "VISION_REQUEST_INVALID"
   274	    assert provider.client.responses.calls == 1

   526	        provider.analyze(
   527	            before_image=b"before",

   643	def test_failure_sets_failed_status_and_no_partial_items_saved(client, create_account, create_menu, create_meal, sample_image_file, monkeypatch, db_session_factory):
   644	    student, _, record = _prepare_record_for_analysis(client, create_account, create_menu, create_meal, sample_image_file)
   645	    monkeypatch.setattr(
   646	        "app.services.vision_service.build_vision_provider",
   647	        lambda: DummyProvider(error=GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 요청 시간이 초과되었습니다.", code="VISION_TIMEOUT", status_code=503, detail="request timed out")),
   648	    )
   649	    response = client.post(f"/api/v1/me/meal-records/{record['id']}/analyze", headers=student["headers"])
   650	    assert response.status_code == 503
   651	    assert response.json()["error"]["code"] == "VISION_TIMEOUT"
   652	    session = db_session_factory()
   653	    try:
   654	        from app.models.meal_item_record import MealItemRecord
   655	        from app.models.meal_record import MealRecord
   656	
   657	        stored = session.get(MealRecord, record["id"])
   658	        assert stored.status == "FAILED"
   659	        assert stored.completed_at is None
   660	        assert stored.failure_reason == "GeminiVisionError: request timed out"
   661	        assert session.query(MealItemRecord).filter(MealItemRecord.meal_record_id == record["id"]).count() == 0
   662	    finally:
   663	        session.close()

    12	def _prepare_flow(client, create_account, create_menu, create_meal):
    13	    admin = create_account(login_id="admin1", student_number="90000001", role="ADMIN")
    14	    student = create_account(login_id="student1", student_number="20223137")
    15	    menu = create_menu(admin["headers"])
    16	    meal = create_meal(admin["headers"], [menu["id"]])
    17	    client.post("/api/v1/me/rfid-cards", headers=student["headers"], json={"uid": "04A3B29C7F6180"})
    18	    return student, meal, admin

   101	def test_image_reupload_invalidates_previous_analysis(client, create_account, create_menu, create_meal, sample_image_file, sample_png_file, db_session_factory):
   102	    student, meal, _ = _prepare_flow(client, create_account, create_menu, create_meal)
   103	    record = client.post("/api/v1/device/meal-records", headers={"X-Device-Key": "device-secret"}, json={"rfid_uid": "04A3B29C7F6180", "meal_id": meal["id"]}).json()["data"]
   104	    client.post(f"/api/v1/me/meal-records/{record['id']}/images/before", headers=student["headers"], files={"file": sample_image_file})
   105	    client.post(f"/api/v1/me/meal-records/{record['id']}/images/after", headers=student["headers"], files={"file": sample_image_file})
   106	    analyze = client.post(f"/api/v1/me/meal-records/{record['id']}/analyze", headers=student["headers"])
   107	    assert analyze.status_code == 200
   108	
   109	    session = db_session_factory()
   110	    try:
   111	        stored_record = session.get(MealRecord, record["id"])
   112	        old_before = next(image for image in stored_record.images if image.image_type == "BEFORE")
   113	        old_before_file = Path(settings.UPLOAD_DIR) / old_before.image_url
   114	        assert session.query(MealItemRecord).filter(MealItemRecord.meal_record_id == record["id"]).count() > 0
   115	    finally:
   116	        session.close()
   117	
   118	    replace = client.post(f"/api/v1/me/meal-records/{record['id']}/images/before", headers=student["headers"], files={"file": sample_png_file})
   119	    assert replace.status_code == 201
   120	
   121	    session = db_session_factory()
   122	    try:
   123	        stored_record = session.get(MealRecord, record["id"])
   124	        assert stored_record.status == "IMAGES_UPLOADED"
   125	        assert stored_record.completed_at is None
   126	        assert stored_record.failure_reason is None
   127	        assert session.query(MealItemRecord).filter(MealItemRecord.meal_record_id == record["id"]).count() == 0
   128	    finally:
   129	        session.close()
   130	    assert not old_before_file.exists()

   133	def test_blob_image_access_streaming_response(client, create_account, create_menu, create_meal, sample_image_file, monkeypatch):
   134	    class FakeBlobStorage:
   135	        def build_key(self, *, meal_record_id: int, image_type, filename: str) -> str:
   136	            return f"meal-images/{meal_record_id}/{image_type.value.lower()}/{filename}"
   137	
   138	        def save(self, *, key: str, content: bytes, content_type: str) -> str:
   139	            return key

   200	def test_blob_reupload_deletes_old_blob_after_commit(client, create_account, create_menu, create_meal, sample_image_file, sample_png_file, monkeypatch):
   201	    class FakeBlobStorage:
   202	        def __init__(self):
   203	            self.saved = []
   204	            self.deleted = []
   205	            self._content = {}
   206	
   207	        def build_key(self, *, meal_record_id: int, image_type, filename: str) -> str:
   208	            return f"meal-images/{meal_record_id}/{image_type.value.lower()}/{filename}"
   209	
   210	        def save(self, *, key: str, content: bytes, content_type: str) -> str:
   211	            self.saved.append(key)
   212	            self._content[key] = content
   213	            return key
   214	
   215	        def delete(self, key: str) -> None:
   216	            self.deleted.append(key)
   217	            self._content.pop(key, None)
   218	
   219	        def resolve_local_path(self, key: str):
   220	            return None
   221	
   222	        def read(self, key: str) -> bytes:
   223	            return self._content[key]
   224	
   225	    fake_storage = FakeBlobStorage()
   226	    monkeypatch.setattr("app.services.image_service.build_image_storage", lambda: fake_storage)
   227	    student, meal, _ = _prepare_flow(client, create_account, create_menu, create_meal)
   228	    record = client.post("/api/v1/device/meal-records", headers={"X-Device-Key": "device-secret"}, json={"rfid_uid": "04A3B29C7F6180", "meal_id": meal["id"]}).json()["data"]
   229	    first = client.post(f"/api/v1/me/meal-records/{record['id']}/images/before", headers=student["headers"], files={"file": sample_image_file})
   230	    second = client.post(f"/api/v1/me/meal-records/{record['id']}/images/before", headers=student["headers"], files={"file": sample_png_file})
   231	    assert first.status_code == 201
   232	    assert second.status_code == 201
   233	    assert len(fake_storage.saved) == 2
   234	    assert fake_storage.deleted == [fake_storage.saved[0]]
   235

   265	        warnings.append((message, args, kwargs))

   279	def test_device_meal_record_rejects_yesterday_and_other_school(client, create_account, create_menu, create_meal):
   280	    student, _, admin = _prepare_flow(client, create_account, create_menu, create_meal)
   281	    yesterday_menu = create_menu(admin["headers"], name="어제메뉴")
   282	    yesterday_meal = create_meal(admin["headers"], [yesterday_menu["id"]], meal_date=(today_local() - timedelta(days=1)).isoformat())
   283	    response = client.post("/api/v1/device/meal-records", headers={"X-Device-Key": "device-secret"}, json={"rfid_uid": "04A3B29C7F6180", "meal_id": yesterday_meal["id"]})
   284	    assert response.status_code == 400
   285	    assert response.json()["error"]["code"] == "INVALID_MEAL_DATE"
   286	
   287	    other_school_menu = create_menu(admin["headers"], name="타학교메뉴")
   288	    other_school_meal = create_meal(admin["headers"], [other_school_menu["id"]], school_name="다른학교")
   289	    response = client.post("/api/v1/device/meal-records", headers={"X-Device-Key": "device-secret"}, json={"rfid_uid": "04A3B29C7F6180", "meal_id": other_school_meal["id"]})
   290	    assert response.status_code == 404
   291	    assert response.json()["error"]["code"] == "MEAL_NOT_FOUND"

    15	class FakeBlobError(Exception):
    16	    def __init__(self, status_code: int, message: str = "blob error"):
    17	        super().__init__(message)
    18	        self.status_code = status_code
    19	
    20	
    21	class FakeBlobNotFoundError(Exception):
    22	    pass
    23	
    24	
    25	class FakeBlobAccessError(Exception):
    26	    pass
    27	
    28	
    29	class FakeBlobNoTokenProvidedError(Exception):
    30	    pass
    31	
    32

    34	    pass
    35

    38	    pass

    45	def make_http_status_error(status_code: int):
    46	    request = httpx.Request("GET", "https://example.invalid/blob")
    47	    response = httpx.Response(status_code, request=request)
    48	    return httpx.HTTPStatusError("blob request failed", request=request, response=response)
    49	
    50	
    51	class FakeBlobClient:
    52	    last_instance = None
    53	    NONE = object()
    54	
    55	    def __init__(self, token=None):
    56	        self.token = token
    57	        self.put_calls = []
    58	        self.get_calls = []
    59	        self.head_calls = []
    60	        self.delete_calls = []
    61	        self.closed = False
    62	        self.behavior = {}
    63	        FakeBlobClient.last_instance = self
    64	
    65	    def __enter__(self):
    66	        return self
    67	
    68	    def __exit__(self, exc_type, exc, tb):
    69	        self.closed = True
    70	
    71	    def put(self, pathname, content, *, access, content_type, add_random_suffix, overwrite=False, cache_control_max_age=None, multipart=False, on_upload_progress=None):
    72	        self.put_calls.append(
    73	            {
    74	                "pathname": pathname,
    75	                "content": content,
    76	                "access": access,
    77	                "content_type": content_type,
    78	                "add_random_suffix": add_random_suffix,
    79	                "overwrite": overwrite,
    80	            }
    81	        )
    82	        effect = self.behavior.get("put")
    83	        if isinstance(effect, Exception):
    84	            raise effect
    85	        return effect if effect is not None else SimpleNamespace(pathname=pathname, url="https://store.private.blob.vercel-storage.com/" + pathname)
    86	
    87	    def get(self, target, *, access="public", timeout=None, use_cache=True, if_none_match=None):
    88	        self.get_calls.append(
    89	            {
    90	                "target": target,
    91	                "access": access,
    92	                "timeout": timeout,
    93	                "use_cache": use_cache,
    94	                "if_none_match": if_none_match,
    95	            }
    96	        )
    97	        effect = self.behavior.get("get")
    98	        if isinstance(effect, Exception):
    99	            raise effect
   100	        if effect is self.NONE:
   101	            return None
   102	        return effect if effect is not None else b"image-bytes"
   103	
   104	    def head(self, target):
   105	        self.head_calls.append(target)
   106	        effect = self.behavior.get("head")
   107	        if isinstance(effect, Exception):
   108	            raise effect
   109	        return effect if effect is not None else SimpleNamespace(pathname="meal-images/1/before/test.jpg")
   110	
   111	    def delete(self, target_or_targets):
   112	        self.delete_calls.append(target_or_targets)
   113	        effect = self.behavior.get("delete")
   114	        if isinstance(effect, Exception):
   115	            raise effect
   116	        return effect
   117

   119	def _make_storage(monkeypatch, *, token="token", vercel=False):
   120	    monkeypatch.setattr("app.services.storage.vercel_blob_storage.BlobClient", FakeBlobClient)
   121	    monkeypatch.setattr("app.services.storage.vercel_blob_storage.BlobNotFoundError", FakeBlobNotFoundError)
   122	    monkeypatch.setattr("app.services.storage.vercel_blob_storage.BlobAccessError", FakeBlobAccessError)
   123	    monkeypatch.setattr("app.services.storage.vercel_blob_storage.BlobNoTokenProvidedError", FakeBlobNoTokenProvidedError)
   124	    monkeypatch.setattr("app.services.storage.vercel_blob_storage.BlobServiceNotAvailable", FakeBlobServiceNotAvailable)
   125	    monkeypatch.setattr("app.services.storage.vercel_blob_storage.BlobServiceRateLimited", FakeBlobServiceRateLimited)
   126	    monkeypatch.setattr("app.services.storage.vercel_blob_storage.BlobStoreSuspendedError", FakeBlobStoreSuspendedError)
   127	    monkeypatch.setattr("app.services.storage.vercel_blob_storage.settings.BLOB_STORE_ID", "")
   128	    monkeypatch.setattr("app.services.storage.vercel_blob_storage.settings.BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN", token)
   129	    monkeypatch.setattr("app.services.storage.vercel_blob_storage.settings.VERCEL_OIDC_TOKEN", "oidc-token")
   130	    if vercel:
   131	        monkeypatch.setenv("VERCEL", "1")
   132	    else:
   133	        monkeypatch.delenv("VERCEL", raising=False)
   134	    return VercelBlobStorage()
   135

   380	    error.status_code = 401
   381	    assert VercelBlobStorage._get_status_code(error) == 401

   387	    assert VercelBlobStorage._get_status_code(error) is None

     1	def test_allergen_seed_count_and_codes(client):
     2	    response = client.get("/api/v1/allergens")
     3	    assert response.status_code == 200
     4	    items = response.json()["data"]
     5	    codes = [item["code"] for item in items]
     6	    assert len(items) == 19
     7	    assert "PINE_NUT" in codes
     8	    assert "EGGS" in codes
     9	    assert "SULFITES" in codes
    10	    assert "EGG" not in codes
    11	    assert "SULFITE" not in codes
    12	
    13	
    14	def test_update_my_allergies(client, create_account):
    15	    student = create_account(login_id="student1", student_number="20223137")
    16	    response = client.put("/api/v1/me/allergens", headers=student["headers"], json={"allergen_codes": ["MILK", "SHRIMP", "PINE_NUT"]})
    17	    assert response.status_code == 200
    18	    codes = [item["code"] for item in response.json()["data"]["items"]]
    19	    assert set(codes) == {"MILK", "SHRIMP", "PINE_NUT"}

    22	def test_allergy_intersection_restriction(client, create_account, create_menu, create_meal):
    23	    admin = create_account(login_id="admin1", student_number="90000001", role="ADMIN")
    24	    student = create_account(login_id="student1", student_number="20223137", allergen_codes=["MILK", "PEANUT"])
    25	    menu = create_menu(admin["headers"], name="우유죽", allergen_codes=["MILK"])
    26	    create_meal(admin["headers"], [menu["id"]], meal_type="LUNCH")
    27	    client.post("/api/v1/me/rfid-cards", headers=student["headers"], json={"uid": "04A3B29C7F6180"})
    28	    response = client.post(
    29	        "/api/v1/device/rfid/scan",
    30	        headers={"X-Device-Key": "device-secret"},
    31	        json={"uid": "04A3B29C7F6180", "meal_type": "LUNCH"},
    32	    )
    33	    assert response.status_code == 200
    34	    assert response.json()["data"]["menu_guidance"][0]["is_restricted"] is True

    40	def _get_allergen_id(bind, code: str) -> int | None:
    41	    return bind.execute(sa.text("SELECT id FROM allergens WHERE code = :code"), {"code": code}).scalar()
    42

    44	def _merge_allergen_code(bind, old_code: str, new_code: str) -> None:
    45	    old_id = _get_allergen_id(bind, old_code)
    46	    new_id = _get_allergen_id(bind, new_code)
    47	    if old_id is None:
    48	        return
    49	    if new_id is None:
    50	        bind.execute(sa.text("UPDATE allergens SET code = :new_code WHERE id = :old_id"), {"new_code": new_code, "old_id": old_id})
    51	        return
    52	    if old_id == new_id:
    53	        return
    54	
    55	    bind.execute(
    56	        sa.text(
    57	            """
    58	            UPDATE user_allergies
    59	            SET allergen_id = :new_id
    60	            WHERE allergen_id = :old_id
    61	              AND NOT EXISTS (
    62	                SELECT 1
    63	                FROM user_allergies ua2
    64	                WHERE ua2.user_id = user_allergies.user_id
    65	                  AND ua2.allergen_id = :new_id
    66	              )
    67	            """
    68	        ),
    69	        {"old_id": old_id, "new_id": new_id},
    70	    )
    71	    bind.execute(sa.text("DELETE FROM user_allergies WHERE allergen_id = :old_id"), {"old_id": old_id})
    72	
    73	    bind.execute(
    74	        sa.text(
    75	            """
    76	            UPDATE menu_allergens
    77	            SET allergen_id = :new_id
    78	            WHERE allergen_id = :old_id
    79	              AND NOT EXISTS (
    80	                SELECT 1
    81	                FROM menu_allergens ma2
    82	                WHERE ma2.menu_id = menu_allergens.menu_id
    83	                  AND ma2.allergen_id = :new_id
    84	              )
    85	            """
    86	        ),
    87	        {"old_id": old_id, "new_id": new_id},
    88	    )
    89	    bind.execute(sa.text("DELETE FROM menu_allergens WHERE allergen_id = :old_id"), {"old_id": old_id})
    90	    bind.execute(sa.text("DELETE FROM allergens WHERE id = :old_id"), {"old_id": old_id})

     1	from logging.config import fileConfig
     2	
     3	from alembic import context
     4	from sqlalchemy import engine_from_config, pool
     5	
     6	from app.core.config import settings
     7	from app.core.database import Base
     8	from app.models import *  # noqa: F401,F403
     9	
    10	config = context.config
    11	migration_url = settings.DATABASE_URL_UNPOOLED or settings.DATABASE_URL
    12	config.set_main_option("sqlalchemy.url", migration_url.replace("%", "%%"))
    13	
    14	if config.config_file_name is not None:
    15	    fileConfig(config.config_file_name)
    16	
    17	target_metadata = Base.metadata
    18	
    19	
    20	def run_migrations_offline() -> None:
    21	    context.configure(
    22	        url=config.get_main_option("sqlalchemy.url"),
    23	        target_metadata=target_metadata,
    24	        literal_binds=True,
    25	        compare_type=True,
    26	        render_as_batch=True,
    27	    )
    28	    with context.begin_transaction():
    29	        context.run_migrations()
    30	
    31	
    32	def run_migrations_online() -> None:
    33	    connectable = engine_from_config(
    34	        config.get_section(config.config_ini_section, {}),
    35	        prefix="sqlalchemy.",
    36	        poolclass=pool.NullPool,
    37	    )
    38	    with connectable.connect() as connection:
    39	        context.configure(connection=connection, target_metadata=target_metadata, compare_type=True, render_as_batch=True)
    40	        with context.begin_transaction():
    41	            context.run_migrations()
    42	
    43	
    44	if context.is_offline_mode():
    45	    run_migrations_offline()
    46	else:
    47	    run_migrations_online()

===== FILE: app/services/analysis_service.py =====
     1	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     2	
     3	from app.core.exceptions import AppException, BadRequestException, ConflictException, ForbiddenException
     4	from app.repositories.meal_image_repository import MealImageRepository
     5	from app.repositories.meal_item_record_repository import MealItemRecordRepository
     6	from app.repositories.meal_record_repository import MealRecordRepository
     7	from app.services.storage.factory import build_image_storage
     8	from app.services.vision_service import VisionService
     9	from app.utils.datetime import get_current_utc_datetime
    10	from app.utils.enums import ConsumptionLevel, ImageType, MealRecordStatus
    11	
    12	
    13	class AnalysisService:
    14	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    15	        self.db = db
    16	        self.meal_record_repository = MealRecordRepository(db)
    17	        self.image_repository = MealImageRepository(db)
    18	        self.meal_item_record_repository = MealItemRecordRepository(db)
    19	        self.vision_service = VisionService()
    20	        self.storage = build_image_storage()
    21	
    22	    async def analyze(self, meal_record_id: int, *, user_id: int | None = None, allow_completed: bool = False):
    23	        record = self.meal_record_repository.get_by_id(meal_record_id)
    24	        if not record:
    25	            raise BadRequestException(message="식사 기록을 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="MEAL_RECORD_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"meal_record_id={meal_record_id}")
    26	        if user_id is not None and record.user_id != user_id:
    27	            raise ForbiddenException(message="접근 권한이 없습니다.", code="FORBIDDEN_RESOURCE", detail=f"meal_record_id={meal_record_id}")
    28	        before_image = self.image_repository.get_by_record_and_type(meal_record_id, ImageType.BEFORE)
    29	        after_image = self.image_repository.get_by_record_and_type(meal_record_id, ImageType.AFTER)
    30	        if not before_image:
    31	            raise BadRequestException(message="식전 이미지가 필요합니다.", code="BEFORE_IMAGE_REQUIRED", detail="before image missing")
    32	        if not after_image:
    33	            raise BadRequestException(message="식후 이미지가 필요합니다.", code="AFTER_IMAGE_REQUIRED", detail="after image missing")
    34	
    35	        if record.status == MealRecordStatus.COMPLETED and not allow_completed:
    36	            existing_items = self.meal_item_record_repository.list_by_record(meal_record_id)
    37	            existing_type = existing_items[0].analysis_type if existing_items else self.vision_service.current_analysis_type()
    38	            return existing_items, existing_type, "메뉴별 섭취율 분석 결과입니다."
    39	        if allow_completed and any(item.is_corrected for item in record.item_records):
    40	            raise ConflictException(message="보정된 결과가 있어 재분석할 수 없습니다.", code="CORRECTED_RESULT_EXISTS", detail=f"meal_record_id={meal_record_id}")
    41	
    42	        allowed_statuses = [MealRecordStatus.IMAGES_UPLOADED, MealRecordStatus.FAILED]
    43	        if allow_completed:
    44	            allowed_statuses.append(MealRecordStatus.COMPLETED)
    45	        claimed = self.meal_record_repository.claim_for_analysis(meal_record_id, allowed_statuses=allowed_statuses)
    46	        if claimed == 0:
    47	            refreshed = self.meal_record_repository.get_by_id(meal_record_id)
    48	            if refreshed and refreshed.status == MealRecordStatus.ANALYZING:
    49	                raise ConflictException(message="이미 분석 중입니다.", code="ANALYSIS_ALREADY_RUNNING", detail=f"meal_record_id={meal_record_id}")
    50	            if refreshed and refreshed.status == MealRecordStatus.COMPLETED and not allow_completed:
    51	                existing_items = self.meal_item_record_repository.list_by_record(meal_record_id)
    52	                existing_type = existing_items[0].analysis_type if existing_items else self.vision_service.current_analysis_type()
    53	                return existing_items, existing_type, "메뉴별 섭취율 분석 결과입니다."
    54	            raise ConflictException(message="현재 상태에서는 분석할 수 없습니다.", code="INVALID_ANALYSIS_STATE", detail=f"status={refreshed.status if refreshed else 'UNKNOWN'}")
    55	        self.db.commit()
    56	
    57	        try:
    58	            menu_items = [
    59	                {
    60	                    "meal_menu_item_id": item.id,
    61	                    "menu_id": item.menu_id,
    62	                    "menu_name": item.menu.name,
    63	                }
    64	                for item in record.meal.meal_menu_items
    65	            ]
    66	            analysis_type, result = await self.vision_service.analyze(
    67	                before_image=self.storage.read(before_image.image_url),
    68	                before_mime_type=before_image.mime_type,
    69	                after_image=self.storage.read(after_image.image_url),
    70	                after_mime_type=after_image.mime_type,
    71	                menu_items=menu_items,
    72	            )
    73	            self._validate_result(menu_items, result.items)
    74	            if allow_completed:
    75	                self.meal_item_record_repository.delete_by_record(meal_record_id)
    76	            for item in result.items:
    77	                existing = self.meal_item_record_repository.get_by_record_and_meal_menu_item(meal_record_id, item.meal_menu_item_id)
    78	                self.meal_item_record_repository.create_or_update(
    79	                    existing,
    80	                    meal_record_id=meal_record_id,
    81	                    meal_menu_item_id=item.meal_menu_item_id,
    82	                    consumed_ratio=item.consumed_ratio,
    83	                    consumption_level=self._level(item.consumed_ratio),
    84	                    confidence=item.confidence,
    85	                    is_corrected=False,
    86	                    corrected_at=None,
    87	                    corrected_by=None,
    88	                    note=item.note,
    89	                    analysis_type=analysis_type,
    90	                )
    91	            self.meal_record_repository.update_status(
    92	                self.meal_record_repository.get_by_id(meal_record_id),
    93	                status=MealRecordStatus.COMPLETED,
    94	                completed_at=get_current_utc_datetime(),
    95	                failure_reason=None,
    96	            )
    97	            self.db.commit()
    98	            return self.meal_item_record_repository.list_by_record(meal_record_id), analysis_type, result.analysis_note
    99	        except Exception as exc:
   100	            self.db.rollback()
   101	            failed_record = self.meal_record_repository.get_by_id(meal_record_id)
   102	            self.meal_record_repository.update_status(
   103	                failed_record,
   104	                status=MealRecordStatus.FAILED,
   105	                completed_at=None,
   106	                failure_reason=self._safe_failure_reason(exc),
   107	            )
   108	            self.db.commit()
   109	            raise
   110	
   111	    async def reanalyze(self, meal_record_id: int, *, user_id: int):
   112	        return await self.analyze(meal_record_id, user_id=user_id, allow_completed=True)
   113	
   114	    def correct_consumed_ratio(self, meal_item_record_id: int, user_id: int, consumed_ratio: float):
   115	        item_record = self.meal_item_record_repository.get_by_id(meal_item_record_id)
   116	        if not item_record:
   117	            raise BadRequestException(message="분석 항목을 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="MEAL_RECORD_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"meal_item_record_id={meal_item_record_id}")
   118	        if item_record.meal_record.user_id != user_id:
   119	            raise ForbiddenException(message="접근 권한이 없습니다.", code="FORBIDDEN_RESOURCE", detail=f"meal_item_record_id={meal_item_record_id}")
   120	        if not 0.0 <= consumed_ratio <= 1.0:
   121	            raise BadRequestException(message="섭취율 값이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="INVALID_CONSUMED_RATIO", detail=str(consumed_ratio))
   122	        self.meal_item_record_repository.create_or_update(
   123	            item_record,
   124	            meal_record_id=item_record.meal_record_id,
   125	            meal_menu_item_id=item_record.meal_menu_item_id,
   126	            consumed_ratio=consumed_ratio,
   127	            consumption_level=self._level(consumed_ratio),
   128	            confidence=None,
   129	            is_corrected=True,
   130	            corrected_at=get_current_utc_datetime(),
   131	            corrected_by=user_id,
   132	            note=item_record.note,
   133	            analysis_type=item_record.analysis_type,
   134	        )
   135	        self.db.commit()
   136	        return self.meal_item_record_repository.get_by_id(meal_item_record_id)
   137	
   138	    @staticmethod
   139	    def _validate_result(menu_items: list[dict], items: list) -> None:
   140	        expected_ids = {item["meal_menu_item_id"] for item in menu_items}
   141	        expected_pairs = {item["meal_menu_item_id"]: item for item in menu_items}
   142	        actual_ids = [item.meal_menu_item_id for item in items]
   143	        if len(actual_ids) != len(expected_ids):
   144	            raise BadRequestException(message="VLM 응답 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="VLM_MENU_MISSING", detail="menu count mismatch")
   145	        if not actual_ids:
   146	            raise BadRequestException(message="VLM 응답 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="INVALID_VLM_RESPONSE", detail="items is empty")
   147	        if len(set(actual_ids)) != len(actual_ids):
   148	            raise BadRequestException(message="VLM 응답 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="VLM_DUPLICATE_MENU", detail="duplicate meal_menu_item_id")
   149	        if set(actual_ids) != expected_ids:
   150	            raise BadRequestException(message="VLM 응답 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="VLM_MENU_MISSING", detail="missing menu item")
   151	        for item in items:
   152	            source = expected_pairs[item.meal_menu_item_id]
   153	            if item.menu_id != source["menu_id"]:
   154	                raise BadRequestException(message="VLM 응답 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="INVALID_VLM_RESPONSE", detail="menu_id mismatch")
   155	            if not 0.0 <= item.consumed_ratio <= 1.0:
   156	                raise BadRequestException(message="VLM 응답 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="VLM_INVALID_RATIO", detail="consumed_ratio out of range")
   157	            if not 0.0 <= item.confidence <= 1.0:
   158	                raise BadRequestException(message="VLM 응답 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="INVALID_VLM_RESPONSE", detail="confidence out of range")
   159	
   160	    @staticmethod
   161	    def _level(ratio: float) -> ConsumptionLevel:
   162	        if ratio < 0.10:
   163	            return ConsumptionLevel.NONE
   164	        if ratio < 0.40:
   165	            return ConsumptionLevel.LITTLE
   166	        if ratio < 0.70:
   167	            return ConsumptionLevel.HALF
   168	        if ratio < 0.95:
   169	            return ConsumptionLevel.MOST
   170	        return ConsumptionLevel.ALL
   171	
   172	    @staticmethod
   173	    def _safe_failure_reason(exc: Exception) -> str:
   174	        detail = exc.detail if isinstance(exc, AppException) and exc.detail else str(exc)
   175	        if len(detail) > 200:
   176	            detail = detail[:200]
   177	        return f"{type(exc).__name__}: {detail}"

===== FILE: app/services/menu_service.py =====
     1	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     2	
     3	from app.core.exceptions import BadRequestException, ConflictException, NotFoundException
     4	from app.models.menu_allergen import MenuAllergen
     5	from app.models.menu_ingredient import MenuIngredient
     6	from app.repositories.allergen_repository import AllergenRepository
     7	from app.repositories.menu_repository import MenuRepository
     8	from app.schemas.menu import MenuCreateRequest, MenuUpdateRequest
     9	from app.utils.normalization import normalize_allergen_codes, normalize_ingredient_names
    10	
    11	
    12	class MenuService:
    13	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    14	        self.db = db
    15	        self.menu_repository = MenuRepository(db)
    16	        self.allergen_repository = AllergenRepository(db)
    17	
    18	    def create_menu(self, request: MenuCreateRequest):
    19	        if self.menu_repository.get_by_name(request.name):
    20	            raise ConflictException(message="이미 등록된 메뉴입니다.", code="DUPLICATE_MENU_NAME", detail=request.name)
    21	        normalized_ingredients = normalize_ingredient_names(request.ingredients)
    22	        normalized_allergen_codes = normalize_allergen_codes(request.allergen_codes)
    23	        try:
    24	            menu = self.menu_repository.create(
    25	                name=request.name,
    26	                standard_serving_g=request.standard_serving_g,
    27	                calories_per_100g=request.nutrition_per_100g.calories_kcal,
    28	                carbohydrate_per_100g=request.nutrition_per_100g.carbohydrate_g,
    29	                protein_per_100g=request.nutrition_per_100g.protein_g,
    30	                fat_per_100g=request.nutrition_per_100g.fat_g,
    31	                is_active=True,
    32	            )
    33	            self._replace_links(menu, normalized_ingredients, normalized_allergen_codes)
    34	            self.db.commit()
    35	            return self.get_menu(menu.id)
    36	        except Exception:
    37	            self.db.rollback()
    38	            raise
    39	
    40	    def _replace_links(self, menu, ingredients: list[str] | None, allergen_codes: list[str] | None) -> None:
    41	        if ingredients is not None:
    42	            menu.ingredients.clear()
    43	            self.db.flush()
    44	            for name in ingredients:
    45	                ingredient = self.menu_repository.get_or_create_ingredient(name)
    46	                menu.ingredients.append(MenuIngredient(menu_id=menu.id, ingredient_id=ingredient.id))
    47	        if allergen_codes is not None:
    48	            menu.allergens.clear()
    49	            self.db.flush()
    50	            allergens = self.allergen_repository.get_by_codes(allergen_codes)
    51	            if len(allergens) != len(set(allergen_codes)):
    52	                raise BadRequestException(message="유효하지 않은 알레르기 코드가 있습니다.", code="INVALID_ALLERGEN_CODE", detail="unknown allergen code")
    53	            for allergen in allergens:
    54	                menu.allergens.append(MenuAllergen(menu_id=menu.id, allergen_id=allergen.id))
    55	
    56	    def get_menu(self, menu_id: int):
    57	        menu = self.menu_repository.get_by_id(menu_id)
    58	        if not menu:
    59	            raise NotFoundException(message="메뉴를 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="MENU_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"menu_id={menu_id}")
    60	        return menu
    61	
    62	    def list_menus(self, *, include_inactive: bool = False):
    63	        return self.menu_repository.list(include_inactive=include_inactive)
    64	
    65	    def update_menu(self, menu_id: int, request: MenuUpdateRequest):
    66	        menu = self.get_menu(menu_id)
    67	        payload = {}
    68	        if request.name is not None:
    69	            duplicate = self.menu_repository.get_by_name(request.name)
    70	            if duplicate and duplicate.id != menu_id:
    71	                raise ConflictException(message="이미 등록된 메뉴입니다.", code="DUPLICATE_MENU_NAME", detail=request.name)
    72	            payload["name"] = request.name
    73	        if request.standard_serving_g is not None:
    74	            payload["standard_serving_g"] = request.standard_serving_g
    75	        if request.is_active is not None:
    76	            payload["is_active"] = request.is_active
    77	        if request.nutrition_per_100g is not None:
    78	            payload.update(
    79	                calories_per_100g=request.nutrition_per_100g.calories_kcal,
    80	                carbohydrate_per_100g=request.nutrition_per_100g.carbohydrate_g,
    81	                protein_per_100g=request.nutrition_per_100g.protein_g,
    82	                fat_per_100g=request.nutrition_per_100g.fat_g,
    83	            )
    84	        try:
    85	            self.menu_repository.update(menu, **payload)
    86	            normalized_ingredients = normalize_ingredient_names(request.ingredients) if request.ingredients is not None else None
    87	            normalized_allergen_codes = normalize_allergen_codes(request.allergen_codes) if request.allergen_codes is not None else None
    88	            self._replace_links(menu, normalized_ingredients, normalized_allergen_codes)
    89	            self.db.commit()
    90	            return self.get_menu(menu.id)
    91	        except Exception:
    92	            self.db.rollback()
    93	            raise
    94	
    95	    def delete_menu(self, menu_id: int) -> None:
    96	        menu = self.get_menu(menu_id)
    97	        self.menu_repository.deactivate(menu)
    98	        self.db.commit()

     8	class RfidService:
     9	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    10	        self.db = db
    11	        self.rfid_repository = RfidRepository(db)
    12	        self.user_repository = UserRepository(db)
    13	
    14	    def register_my_card(self, user_id: int, uid: str):
    15	        if self.rfid_repository.get_by_uid(uid):
    16	            raise ConflictException(message="이미 등록된 RFID UID입니다.", code="RFID_ALREADY_REGISTERED", detail=uid)
    17	        card = self.rfid_repository.create(user_id=user_id, uid=uid)
    18	        self.db.commit()
    19	        self.db.refresh(card)
    20	        return card
    21	
    22	    def get_active_card_by_uid(self, uid: str):
    23	        card = self.rfid_repository.get_active_by_uid(uid)
    24	        if not card:
    25	            raise NotFoundException(message="RFID 카드를 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="RFID_NOT_FOUND", detail=uid)
    26	        return card
    27	
    28	    def get_scan_ready_card_by_uid(self, uid: str):
    29	        card = self.rfid_repository.get_by_uid(uid)
    30	        if not card:
    31	            raise NotFoundException(message="RFID 카드를 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="RFID_NOT_FOUND", detail=uid)
    32	        if not card.is_active:
    33	            raise BadRequestException(message="비활성 RFID 카드입니다.", code="INACTIVE_RFID_CARD", detail=uid)
    34	        if not card.user.is_active:
    35	            raise UnauthorizedException(message="비활성화된 계정입니다.", code="INACTIVE_USER", detail=f"user_id={card.user_id}")
    36	        return card
    37	
    38	    def list_my_cards(self, user_id: int):
    39	        return self.rfid_repository.list_by_user(user_id)
    40	
    41	    def deactivate_my_card(self, user_id: int, card_id: int):
    42	        card = self.rfid_repository.get_by_id(card_id)
    43	        if not card:
    44	            raise NotFoundException(message="RFID 카드를 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="RFID_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"card_id={card_id}")
    45	        if card.user_id != user_id:
    46	            raise ForbiddenException(message="접근 권한이 없습니다.", code="FORBIDDEN_RESOURCE", detail=f"card_id={card_id}")
    47	        card.is_active = False
    48	        self.db.commit()
    49	        self.db.refresh(card)
    50	        return card

===== FILE: app/services/meal_record_service.py =====
     1	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     2	
     3	from app.core.config import settings
     4	from app.core.exceptions import BadRequestException, ConflictException, ForbiddenException, NotFoundException, UnauthorizedException
     5	from app.repositories.meal_image_repository import MealImageRepository
     6	from app.repositories.meal_item_record_repository import MealItemRecordRepository
     7	from app.repositories.recommendation_repository import RecommendationRepository
     8	from app.repositories.meal_record_repository import MealRecordRepository
     9	from app.repositories.meal_repository import MealRepository
    10	from app.repositories.rfid_repository import RfidRepository
    11	from app.repositories.user_repository import UserRepository
    12	from app.utils.datetime import get_current_date, get_current_utc_datetime, get_recent_start_date
    13	from app.utils.enums import ImageType, MealRecordStatus
    14	
    15	
    16	class MealRecordService:
    17	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    18	        self.db = db
    19	        self.meal_record_repository = MealRecordRepository(db)
    20	        self.meal_image_repository = MealImageRepository(db)
    21	        self.meal_item_record_repository = MealItemRecordRepository(db)
    22	        self.rfid_repository = RfidRepository(db)
    23	        self.meal_repository = MealRepository(db)
    24	        self.user_repository = UserRepository(db)
    25	        self.recommendation_repository = RecommendationRepository(db)
    26	
    27	    def create_from_rfid(self, *, rfid_uid: str, meal_id: int):
    28	        card = self.rfid_repository.get_by_uid(rfid_uid)
    29	        if not card:
    30	            raise NotFoundException(message="RFID 카드를 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="RFID_NOT_FOUND", detail=rfid_uid)
    31	        if not card.is_active:
    32	            raise BadRequestException(message="비활성 RFID 카드입니다.", code="INACTIVE_RFID_CARD", detail=rfid_uid)
    33	        if not card.user.is_active:
    34	            raise UnauthorizedException(message="비활성화된 계정입니다.", code="INACTIVE_USER", detail=f"user_id={card.user_id}")
    35	        meal = self.meal_repository.get_by_id(meal_id)
    36	        if not meal:
    37	            raise NotFoundException(message="급식을 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="MEAL_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"meal_id={meal_id}")
    38	        if meal.school_name != settings.SCHOOL_NAME:
    39	            raise NotFoundException(message="급식을 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="MEAL_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"meal_id={meal_id}")
    40	        if meal.meal_date != get_current_date():
    41	            raise BadRequestException(message="오늘 급식만 기록할 수 있습니다.", code="INVALID_MEAL_DATE", detail=str(meal.meal_date))
    42	        if self.meal_record_repository.get_by_user_and_meal(user_id=card.user_id, meal_id=meal_id):
    43	            raise ConflictException(message="이미 생성된 식사 기록입니다.", code="MEAL_RECORD_ALREADY_EXISTS", detail="duplicate meal record")
    44	        record = self.meal_record_repository.create(user_id=card.user_id, meal_id=meal_id)
    45	        self.db.commit()
    46	        return self.get_record(record.id)
    47	
    48	    def get_record(self, meal_record_id: int):
    49	        record = self.meal_record_repository.get_by_id(meal_record_id)
    50	        if not record:
    51	            raise NotFoundException(message="식사 기록을 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="MEAL_RECORD_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"meal_record_id={meal_record_id}")
    52	        return record
    53	
    54	    def assert_owner(self, meal_record_id: int, user_id: int):
    55	        record = self.get_record(meal_record_id)
    56	        if record.user_id != user_id:
    57	            raise ForbiddenException(message="접근 권한이 없습니다.", code="FORBIDDEN_RESOURCE", detail=f"meal_record_id={meal_record_id}")
    58	        return record
    59	
    60	    def list_recent(self, user_id: int, days: int):
    61	        days = min(max(days, 1), 30)
    62	        end_date = get_current_date()
    63	        start_date = get_recent_start_date(days)
    64	        records = self.meal_record_repository.list_recent_completed_by_user(user_id=user_id, start_date=start_date, end_date=end_date)
    65	        return start_date, end_date, records
    66	
    67	    def recalculate_status_after_image_change(self, meal_record_id: int):
    68	        record = self.get_record(meal_record_id)
    69	        status = self._calculate_status_from_db_images(meal_record_id)
    70	        self.meal_record_repository.update_status(record, status=status, completed_at=None, failure_reason=None)
    71	        self.meal_item_record_repository.delete_by_record(meal_record_id)
    72	        self.recommendation_repository.delete_by_user_and_meal(user_id=record.user_id, meal_id=record.meal_id)
    73	        self.db.flush()
    74	        return record
    75	
    76	    def mark_analyzing(self, meal_record_id: int):
    77	        record = self.get_record(meal_record_id)
    78	        if record.status == MealRecordStatus.ANALYZING:
    79	            raise ConflictException(message="이미 분석 중입니다.", code="ANALYSIS_ALREADY_RUNNING", detail=f"meal_record_id={meal_record_id}")
    80	        self.meal_record_repository.update_status(record, status=MealRecordStatus.ANALYZING)
    81	        self.db.commit()
    82	
    83	    def mark_completed(self, meal_record_id: int):
    84	        record = self.get_record(meal_record_id)
    85	        self.meal_record_repository.update_status(record, status=MealRecordStatus.COMPLETED, completed_at=get_current_utc_datetime(), failure_reason=None)
    86	        self.db.commit()
    87	
    88	    def mark_failed(self, meal_record_id: int):
    89	        record = self.get_record(meal_record_id)
    90	        self.meal_record_repository.update_status(record, status=MealRecordStatus.FAILED)
    91	        self.db.commit()
    92	
    93	    def list_all(self):
    94	        return self.meal_record_repository.list_all()
    95	
    96	    def _calculate_status_from_db_images(self, meal_record_id: int) -> MealRecordStatus:
    97	        has_before = self.meal_image_repository.has_image_type(meal_record_id, ImageType.BEFORE)
    98	        has_after = self.meal_image_repository.has_image_type(meal_record_id, ImageType.AFTER)
    99	        if has_before and has_after:
   100	            return MealRecordStatus.IMAGES_UPLOADED
   101	        if has_before:
   102	            return MealRecordStatus.BEFORE_IMAGE_UPLOADED
   103	        return MealRecordStatus.CREATED

===== FILE: app/services/meal_service.py =====
     1	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     2	
     3	from app.core.config import settings
     4	from app.core.exceptions import BadRequestException, ConflictException, NotFoundException
     5	from app.models.meal_menu_item import MealMenuItem
     6	from app.repositories.meal_repository import MealRepository
     7	from app.repositories.menu_repository import MenuRepository
     8	from app.schemas.meal import MealCreateRequest
     9	
    10	
    11	class MealService:
    12	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    13	        self.db = db
    14	        self.meal_repository = MealRepository(db)
    15	        self.menu_repository = MenuRepository(db)
    16	
    17	    def create_meal(self, request: MealCreateRequest):
    18	        if self.meal_repository.get_by_unique_fields(
    19	            meal_date=request.meal_date,
    20	            meal_type=request.meal_type,
    21	            school_name=request.school_name,
    22	        ):
    23	            raise ConflictException(message="동일한 급식이 이미 존재합니다.", code="DUPLICATE_MEAL", detail="duplicate meal")
    24	        if len(set(request.menu_ids)) != len(request.menu_ids):
    25	            raise BadRequestException(message="중복된 메뉴 ID가 포함되어 있습니다.", code="DUPLICATE_MENU_ID", detail="menu_ids contains duplicates")
    26	        try:
    27	            meal = self.meal_repository.create(
    28	                meal_date=request.meal_date,
    29	                meal_type=request.meal_type,
    30	                school_name=request.school_name,
    31	            )
    32	            for menu_id in request.menu_ids:
    33	                menu = self.menu_repository.get_by_id(menu_id)
    34	                if not menu:
    35	                    raise NotFoundException(message="메뉴를 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="MENU_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"menu_id={menu_id}")
    36	                if not menu.is_active:
    37	                    raise BadRequestException(message="비활성 메뉴는 급식에 등록할 수 없습니다.", code="MENU_INACTIVE", detail=f"menu_id={menu_id}")
    38	                self.db.add(MealMenuItem(meal_id=meal.id, menu_id=menu_id))
    39	            self.db.commit()
    40	            return self.get_meal(meal.id)
    41	        except Exception:
    42	            self.db.rollback()
    43	            raise
    44	
    45	    def get_meal(self, meal_id: int):
    46	        meal = self.meal_repository.get_by_id(meal_id)
    47	        if not meal:
    48	            raise NotFoundException(message="급식을 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="MEAL_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"meal_id={meal_id}")
    49	        return meal
    50	
    51	    def get_today_meals(self):

     1	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     2	
     3	from app.core.exceptions import ConflictException, NotFoundException
     4	from app.repositories.user_repository import UserRepository
     5	from app.schemas.user import UserUpdateRequest
     6	
     7	
     8	class UserService:
     9	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    10	        self.db = db
    11	        self.user_repository = UserRepository(db)
    12	
    13	    def get_user(self, user_id: int):
    14	        user = self.user_repository.get_by_id(user_id)
    15	        if not user:
    16	            raise NotFoundException(message="사용자를 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="USER_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"user_id={user_id}")
    17	        return user
    18	
    19	    def update_me(self, user_id: int, request: UserUpdateRequest):
    20	        user = self.get_user(user_id)
    21	        if request.login_id and request.login_id != user.login_id:
    22	            if self.user_repository.get_by_login_id(request.login_id):
    23	                raise ConflictException(message="이미 사용 중인 로그인 ID입니다.", code="DUPLICATE_LOGIN_ID", detail=request.login_id)
    24	        payload = request.model_dump(exclude_unset=True)
    25	        self.user_repository.update(user, **payload)
    26	        self.db.commit()
    27	        self.db.refresh(user)
    28	        return user
    29	
    30	    def list_active_students(self):
    31	        return self.user_repository.list_active_students()
    32	
    33	    def list_users(self, *, page: int, size: int, keyword: str | None, is_active: bool | None):
    34	        return self.user_repository.list_users(page=page, size=size, keyword=keyword, is_active=is_active)

===== FILE: app/services/image_service.py =====
     1	import logging
     2	
     3	from fastapi import UploadFile
     4	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     5	
     6	from app.core.exceptions import BadRequestException, ForbiddenException, NotFoundException
     7	from app.repositories.meal_image_repository import MealImageRepository
     8	from app.repositories.meal_record_repository import MealRecordRepository
     9	from app.services.meal_record_service import MealRecordService
    10	from app.services.storage.factory import build_image_storage
    11	from app.utils.enums import ImageType
    12	from app.utils.files import (
    13	    generate_filename_for_extension,
    14	    read_upload_file,
    15	)
    16	
    17	logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    18	
    19	
    20	class ImageService:
    21	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    22	        self.db = db
    23	        self.image_repository = MealImageRepository(db)
    24	        self.meal_record_repository = MealRecordRepository(db)
    25	        self.meal_record_service = MealRecordService(db)
    26	        self.storage = build_image_storage()
    27	
    28	    def upload_image(self, meal_record_id: int, image_type: ImageType, file: UploadFile):
    29	        record = self.meal_record_repository.get_by_id(meal_record_id)
    30	        if not record:
    31	            raise NotFoundException(message="식사 기록을 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="MEAL_RECORD_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"meal_record_id={meal_record_id}")
    32	        file_bytes, mime_type, extension = read_upload_file(file)
    33	        existing = self.image_repository.get_by_record_and_type(meal_record_id, image_type)
    34	        old_key = existing.image_url if existing else None
    35	        generated_name = generate_filename_for_extension(extension)
    36	        storage_key = self.storage.build_key(meal_record_id=meal_record_id, image_type=image_type, filename=generated_name)
    37	        saved_key = ""
    38	        try:
    39	            saved_key = self.storage.save(key=storage_key, content=file_bytes, content_type=mime_type)
    40	            image = self.image_repository.create_or_replace(
    41	                existing,
    42	                meal_record_id=meal_record_id,
    43	                image_type=image_type,
    44	                image_url=saved_key,
    45	                mime_type=mime_type,
    46	                file_size=len(file_bytes),
    47	            )
    48	            self.meal_record_service.recalculate_status_after_image_change(meal_record_id)
    49	            self.db.commit()
    50	            if old_key and old_key != saved_key:
    51	                self._delete_storage_key_quietly(old_key, meal_record_id=meal_record_id, image_type=image_type)
    52	            self.db.refresh(image)
    53	            return image
    54	        except Exception:
    55	            self.db.rollback()
    56	            if saved_key:
    57	                self._delete_storage_key_quietly(saved_key, meal_record_id=meal_record_id, image_type=image_type)
    58	            raise
    59	
    60	    def list_images(self, meal_record_id: int):
    61	        return self.image_repository.list_by_record(meal_record_id)
    62	
    63	    def get_image_for_user(self, image_id: int, user_id: int, is_admin: bool = False):
    64	        image = self.image_repository.get_by_id(image_id)
    65	        if not image:
    66	            raise NotFoundException(message="이미지를 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="IMAGE_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"image_id={image_id}")
    67	        if not is_admin and image.meal_record.user_id != user_id:
    68	            raise ForbiddenException(message="접근 권한이 없습니다.", code="FORBIDDEN_RESOURCE", detail=f"image_id={image_id}")
    69	        return image
    70	
    71	    def resolve_image_path(self, image):
    72	        path = self.storage.resolve_local_path(image.image_url)
    73	        if path is not None and not path.exists():
    74	            raise NotFoundException(message="이미지 파일을 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="IMAGE_FILE_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"image_id={image.id}")
    75	        return path
    76	
    77	    def read_image_bytes(self, image) -> bytes:
    78	        return self.storage.read(image.image_url)
    79	
    80	    def _delete_storage_key_quietly(self, key: str, *, meal_record_id: int, image_type: ImageType) -> None:
    81	        try:
    82	            self.storage.delete(key)
    83	        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
    84	            code = getattr(exc, "code", type(exc).__name__)
    85	            logger.warning(
    86	                "failed_to_delete_image_storage_object backend=%s operation=delete meal_record_id=%s image_type=%s error_code=%s",
    87	                getattr(self.storage, "backend_name", "UNKNOWN"),
    88	                meal_record_id,
    89	                image_type.value,
    90	                code,
    91	            )
    92	            return

===== FILE: app/services/recommendation_service.py =====
     1	from statistics import mean
     2	
     3	from sqlalchemy import func, select
     4	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     5	
     6	from app.core.exceptions import NotFoundException
     7	from app.models.meal import Meal
     8	from app.models.meal_item_record import MealItemRecord
     9	from app.models.meal_menu_item import MealMenuItem
    10	from app.models.meal_record import MealRecord
    11	from app.models.serving_recommendation import ServingRecommendation
    12	from app.models.user import User
    13	from app.repositories.meal_item_record_repository import MealItemRecordRepository
    14	from app.repositories.meal_record_repository import MealRecordRepository
    15	from app.repositories.meal_repository import MealRepository
    16	from app.repositories.recommendation_repository import RecommendationRepository
    17	from app.utils.datetime import get_current_date, get_recent_start_date
    18	from app.utils.enums import RecommendationLevel, UserRole
    19	
    20	
    21	class RecommendationService:
    22	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    23	        self.db = db
    24	        self.meal_repository = MealRepository(db)
    25	        self.meal_item_record_repository = MealItemRecordRepository(db)
    26	        self.meal_record_repository = MealRecordRepository(db)
    27	        self.recommendation_repository = RecommendationRepository(db)
    28	
    29	    def generate_for_meal(self, *, user_id: int, meal_id: int):
    30	        meal = self.meal_repository.get_by_id(meal_id)
    31	        if not meal:
    32	            raise NotFoundException(message="급식을 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="MEAL_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"meal_id={meal_id}")
    33	        start_date = get_recent_start_date(5)
    34	        end_date = get_current_date()
    35	        items = []
    36	        for meal_menu_item in meal.meal_menu_items:
    37	            recent = self.meal_item_record_repository.list_recent_same_menu_records(
    38	                user_id=user_id,
    39	                menu_id=meal_menu_item.menu_id,
    40	                start_date=start_date,
    41	                end_date=end_date,
    42	                exclude_meal_id=meal_id,
    43	            )
    44	            ratios = [item.consumed_ratio for item in recent]
    45	            if not ratios:
    46	                level = RecommendationLevel.NORMAL
    47	                ratio = 1.0
    48	                avg_ratio = None
    49	                reason = "이전 섭취 기록이 없어 기준 제공량을 추천합니다."
    50	            else:
    51	                avg_ratio = round(mean(ratios), 2)
    52	                if avg_ratio < 0.50:
    53	                    level = RecommendationLevel.LESS
    54	                    ratio = 0.6
    55	                elif avg_ratio < 0.70:
    56	                    level = RecommendationLevel.LESS
    57	                    ratio = 0.8
    58	                else:
    59	                    level = RecommendationLevel.NORMAL
    60	                    ratio = 1.0
    61	                if len(ratios) == 1:
    62	                    reason = "최근 데이터가 1건뿐이므로 참고용 추천입니다."
    63	                else:
    64	                    reason = f"최근 5일 동일 메뉴 평균 섭취율이 {round(avg_ratio * 100, 2)}%입니다."
    65	            items.append(
    66	                ServingRecommendation(
    67	                    user_id=user_id,
    68	                    meal_id=meal_id,
    69	                    meal_menu_item_id=meal_menu_item.id,
    70	                    recommendation_level=level,
    71	                    recommended_serving_ratio=ratio,
    72	                    recommended_serving_g=round(meal_menu_item.menu.standard_serving_g * ratio, 2),
    73	                    recent_average_consumed_ratio=avg_ratio,
    74	                    sample_count=len(ratios),
    75	                    reason=reason,
    76	                )
    77	            )
    78	        self.recommendation_repository.replace_for_meal(user_id=user_id, meal_id=meal_id, items=items)
    79	        self.db.commit()
    80	        return self.recommendation_repository.list_by_user_and_meal(user_id=user_id, meal_id=meal_id)
    81	
    82	    def get_dashboard(self, target_date):
    83	        active_user_count = self.db.scalar(
    84	            select(func.count(User.id)).where(User.is_active.is_(True), User.role == UserRole.STUDENT)
    85	        ) or 0
    86	        meal_record_count = self.db.scalar(
    87	            select(func.count(MealRecord.id)).join(Meal, Meal.id == MealRecord.meal_id).where(Meal.meal_date == target_date)
    88	        ) or 0
    89	        completed_analysis_count = self.db.scalar(
    90	            select(func.count(MealRecord.id)).join(Meal, Meal.id == MealRecord.meal_id).where(Meal.meal_date == target_date, MealRecord.status == "COMPLETED")
    91	        ) or 0
    92	        failed_analysis_count = self.db.scalar(
    93	            select(func.count(MealRecord.id)).join(Meal, Meal.id == MealRecord.meal_id).where(Meal.meal_date == target_date, MealRecord.status == "FAILED")
    94	        ) or 0
    95	        analysis_sample_count = self.db.scalar(
    96	            select(func.count(MealItemRecord.id))
    97	            .join(MealRecord, MealRecord.id == MealItemRecord.meal_record_id)
    98	            .join(Meal, Meal.id == MealRecord.meal_id)
    99	            .where(Meal.meal_date == target_date, MealRecord.status == "COMPLETED")
   100	        ) or 0
   101	        avg_ratio = self.db.scalar(
   102	            select(func.avg(MealItemRecord.consumed_ratio))
   103	            .join(MealRecord, MealRecord.id == MealItemRecord.meal_record_id)
   104	            .join(Meal, Meal.id == MealRecord.meal_id)
   105	            .where(Meal.meal_date == target_date, MealRecord.status == "COMPLETED")
   106	        )
   107	        avg_ratio_value = round(float(avg_ratio), 2) if avg_ratio is not None else None
   108	        return {
   109	            "date": target_date,
   110	            "active_user_count": int(active_user_count),
   111	            "meal_record_count": int(meal_record_count),
   112	            "completed_analysis_count": int(completed_analysis_count),
   113	            "failed_analysis_count": int(failed_analysis_count),
   114	            "analysis_sample_count": int(analysis_sample_count),
   115	            "average_consumed_ratio": avg_ratio_value,
   116	            "average_leftover_ratio": round(1 - avg_ratio_value, 2) if avg_ratio_value is not None else None,
   117	        }
   118	
   119	    def get_leftover_summary(self, start_date, end_date):
   120	        stmt = (
   121	            select(
   122	                MealMenuItem.menu_id,
   123	                func.min(MealMenuItem.menu_id),
   124	                func.avg(MealItemRecord.consumed_ratio),
   125	                func.count(MealItemRecord.id),
   126	            )
   127	            .join(MealMenuItem, MealMenuItem.id == MealItemRecord.meal_menu_item_id)
   128	            .join(MealRecord, MealRecord.id == MealItemRecord.meal_record_id)
   129	            .join(Meal, Meal.id == MealRecord.meal_id)
   130	            .where(Meal.meal_date >= start_date, Meal.meal_date <= end_date)
   131	            .group_by(MealMenuItem.menu_id)
   132	        )
   133	        result = []
   134	        for menu_id, _, avg_ratio, count in self.db.execute(stmt):
   135	            ratio = round(float(avg_ratio), 2) if avg_ratio is not None else None
   136	            meal_menu_item = self.db.scalar(select(MealMenuItem).where(MealMenuItem.menu_id == menu_id))
   137	            result.append(
   138	                {
   139	                    "menu_id": menu_id,
   140	                    "menu_name": meal_menu_item.menu.name if meal_menu_item else str(menu_id),
   141	                    "analysis_count": int(count),
   142	                    "average_consumed_ratio": ratio,
   143	                    "average_leftover_ratio": round(1 - ratio, 2) if ratio is not None else None,
   144	                }
   145	            )
   146	        return result

===== FILE: app/services/nutrition_service.py =====
     1	from app.models.menu import Menu
     2	
     3	
     4	class NutritionService:
     5	    @staticmethod
     6	    def calculate(menu: Menu, consumed_ratio: float) -> dict[str, float | bool]:
     7	        estimated_consumed_g = round(menu.standard_serving_g * consumed_ratio, 2)
     8	        factor = estimated_consumed_g / 100
     9	        return {
    10	            "estimated_consumed_g": estimated_consumed_g,
    11	            "calories_kcal": round(menu.calories_per_100g * factor, 2),
    12	            "carbohydrate_g": round(menu.carbohydrate_per_100g * factor, 2),
    13	            "protein_g": round(menu.protein_per_100g * factor, 2),
    14	            "fat_g": round(menu.fat_per_100g * factor, 2),
    15	            "is_estimated": True,
    16	        }

    16	        return self.allergen_repository.list_active()
    17	
    18	    def get_my_allergies(self, user_id: int):
    19	        user = self.user_repository.get_by_id(user_id)
    20	        return [item.allergen for item in user.allergies]
    21	
    22	    def replace_my_allergies(self, user_id: int, codes: list[str]):

    24	        allergens = self.allergen_repository.get_by_codes(normalized_codes)
    25	        if len(allergens) != len(normalized_codes):
    26	            raise BadRequestException(message="유효하지 않은 알레르기 코드가 있습니다.", code="INVALID_ALLERGEN_CODE", detail="unknown allergen code")
    27	        self.allergen_repository.replace_user_allergies(user_id, [item.id for item in allergens])
    28	        self.db.commit()
    29	        return allergens

===== FILE: app/repositories/auth_repository.py =====
     1	from datetime import datetime
     2	
     3	from sqlalchemy import select, update
     4	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     5	
     6	from app.models.refresh_token import RefreshToken
     7	
     8	
     9	class AuthRepository:
    10	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    11	        self.db = db
    12	
    13	    def create_refresh_token(self, *, user_id: int, token_hash: str, expires_at: datetime) -> RefreshToken:
    14	        token = RefreshToken(user_id=user_id, token_hash=token_hash, expires_at=expires_at)
    15	        self.db.add(token)
    16	        self.db.flush()
    17	        return token
    18	
    19	    def get_refresh_token(self, token_hash: str) -> RefreshToken | None:
    20	        stmt = select(RefreshToken).where(RefreshToken.token_hash == token_hash)
    21	        return self.db.scalar(stmt)
    22	
    23	    def revoke_refresh_token(self, refresh_token: RefreshToken, revoked_at: datetime) -> RefreshToken:
    24	        refresh_token.revoked_at = revoked_at
    25	        self.db.flush()
    26	        return refresh_token
    27	
    28	    def revoke_all_by_user_id(self, user_id: int, revoked_at: datetime) -> None:
    29	        self.db.execute(
    30	            update(RefreshToken)
    31	            .where(RefreshToken.user_id == user_id, RefreshToken.revoked_at.is_(None))
    32	            .values(revoked_at=revoked_at)
    33	        )

===== FILE: app/repositories/recommendation_repository.py =====
     1	from sqlalchemy import delete, select
     2	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session, joinedload
     3	
     4	from app.models.meal_menu_item import MealMenuItem
     5	from app.models.serving_recommendation import ServingRecommendation
     6	
     7	
     8	class RecommendationRepository:
     9	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    10	        self.db = db
    11	
    12	    def replace_for_meal(self, *, user_id: int, meal_id: int, items: list[ServingRecommendation]) -> list[ServingRecommendation]:
    13	        self.db.execute(delete(ServingRecommendation).where(ServingRecommendation.user_id == user_id, ServingRecommendation.meal_id == meal_id))
    14	        for item in items:
    15	            self.db.add(item)
    16	        self.db.flush()
    17	        return items
    18	
    19	    def delete_by_user_and_meal(self, *, user_id: int, meal_id: int) -> None:
    20	        self.db.execute(delete(ServingRecommendation).where(ServingRecommendation.user_id == user_id, ServingRecommendation.meal_id == meal_id))
    21	
    22	    def list_by_user_and_meal(self, *, user_id: int, meal_id: int) -> list[ServingRecommendation]:
    23	        stmt = (
    24	            select(ServingRecommendation)
    25	            .options(joinedload(ServingRecommendation.meal_menu_item).joinedload(MealMenuItem.menu))
    26	            .where(ServingRecommendation.user_id == user_id, ServingRecommendation.meal_id == meal_id)
    27	            .order_by(ServingRecommendation.id.asc())
    28	        )
    29	        return list(self.db.scalars(stmt).all())

===== FILE: app/repositories/user_repository.py =====
     1	from sqlalchemy import func, or_, select
     2	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session, joinedload
     3	
     4	from app.models.user_allergy import UserAllergy
     5	from app.models.user import User
     6	
     7	
     8	class UserRepository:
     9	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    10	        self.db = db
    11	
    12	    def create(self, **kwargs) -> User:
    13	        user = User(**kwargs)
    14	        self.db.add(user)
    15	        self.db.flush()
    16	        return user
    17	
    18	    def get_by_id(self, user_id: int) -> User | None:
    19	        stmt = (
    20	            select(User)
    21	            .options(joinedload(User.allergies).joinedload(UserAllergy.allergen))
    22	            .where(User.id == user_id)
    23	        )
    24	        return self.db.scalars(stmt).unique().one_or_none()
    25	
    26	    def get_by_login_id(self, login_id: str) -> User | None:
    27	        stmt = select(User).where(User.login_id == login_id)
    28	        return self.db.scalar(stmt)
    29	
    30	    def get_by_student_number(self, student_number: str) -> User | None:
    31	        stmt = select(User).where(User.student_number == student_number)
    32	        return self.db.scalar(stmt)
    33	
    34	    def list_active_students(self) -> list[User]:
    35	        stmt = select(User).where(User.is_active.is_(True)).order_by(User.id.asc())
    36	        return list(self.db.scalars(stmt).all())
    37	
    38	    def list_users(self, *, page: int, size: int, keyword: str | None = None, is_active: bool | None = None) -> tuple[list[User], int]:
    39	        stmt = select(User)
    40	        count_stmt = select(func.count(User.id))
    41	        if keyword:
    42	            pattern = f"%{keyword.lower()}%"
    43	            filter_expr = or_(
    44	                func.lower(User.name).like(pattern),
    45	                func.lower(User.login_id).like(pattern),
    46	                func.lower(User.student_number).like(pattern),
    47	            )
    48	            stmt = stmt.where(filter_expr)
    49	            count_stmt = count_stmt.where(filter_expr)
    50	        if is_active is not None:
    51	            stmt = stmt.where(User.is_active.is_(is_active))
    52	            count_stmt = count_stmt.where(User.is_active.is_(is_active))
    53	        total = int(self.db.scalar(count_stmt) or 0)
    54	        items = list(self.db.scalars(stmt.order_by(User.id.asc()).offset((page - 1) * size).limit(size)).all())
    55	        return items, total
    56	
    57	    def update(self, user: User, **kwargs) -> User:
    58	        for key, value in kwargs.items():
    59	            setattr(user, key, value)
    60	        self.db.flush()
    61	        return user

===== FILE: app/repositories/menu_repository.py =====
     1	from sqlalchemy import select
     2	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session, joinedload
     3	
     4	from app.models.ingredient import Ingredient
     5	from app.models.menu import Menu
     6	from app.models.menu_allergen import MenuAllergen
     7	from app.models.menu_ingredient import MenuIngredient
     8	
     9	
    10	class MenuRepository:
    11	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    12	        self.db = db
    13	
    14	    def _query(self):
    15	        return select(Menu).options(
    16	            joinedload(Menu.ingredients).joinedload(MenuIngredient.ingredient),
    17	            joinedload(Menu.allergens).joinedload(MenuAllergen.allergen),
    18	        )
    19	
    20	    def create(self, **kwargs) -> Menu:
    21	        menu = Menu(**kwargs)
    22	        self.db.add(menu)
    23	        self.db.flush()
    24	        return menu
    25	
    26	    def get_by_id(self, menu_id: int) -> Menu | None:
    27	        stmt = self._query().where(Menu.id == menu_id)
    28	        return self.db.scalars(stmt).unique().one_or_none()
    29	
    30	    def get_by_name(self, name: str) -> Menu | None:
    31	        stmt = self._query().where(Menu.name == name)
    32	        return self.db.scalars(stmt).unique().one_or_none()
    33	
    34	    def list(self, *, include_inactive: bool = False) -> list[Menu]:
    35	        stmt = self._query()
    36	        if not include_inactive:
    37	            stmt = stmt.where(Menu.is_active.is_(True))
    38	        stmt = stmt.order_by(Menu.name.asc())
    39	        return list(self.db.scalars(stmt).unique().all())
    40	
    41	    def update(self, menu: Menu, **kwargs) -> Menu:
    42	        for key, value in kwargs.items():
    43	            setattr(menu, key, value)
    44	        self.db.flush()
    45	        return menu
    46	
    47	    def deactivate(self, menu: Menu) -> None:
    48	        menu.is_active = False
    49	        self.db.flush()
    50	
    51	    def get_or_create_ingredient(self, name: str) -> Ingredient:
    52	        stmt = select(Ingredient).where(Ingredient.name == name)
    53	        ingredient = self.db.scalar(stmt)
    54	        if ingredient:
    55	            return ingredient
    56	        ingredient = Ingredient(name=name)
    57	        self.db.add(ingredient)
    58	        self.db.flush()
    59	        return ingredient
