===== FILE: app/repositories/allergen_repository.py =====
     1	from sqlalchemy import select
     2	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     3	
     4	from app.models.allergen import Allergen
     5	from app.models.user_allergy import UserAllergy
     6	
     7	
     8	class AllergenRepository:
     9	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    10	        self.db = db
    11	
    12	    def list_active(self) -> list[Allergen]:
    13	        stmt = select(Allergen).where(Allergen.is_active.is_(True)).order_by(Allergen.display_number.asc())
    14	        return list(self.db.scalars(stmt).all())
    15	
    16	    def get_by_codes(self, codes: list[str]) -> list[Allergen]:
    17	        if not codes:
    18	            return []
    19	        stmt = select(Allergen).where(Allergen.code.in_(codes), Allergen.is_active.is_(True))
    20	        return list(self.db.scalars(stmt).all())
    21	
    22	    def replace_user_allergies(self, user_id: int, allergen_ids: list[int]) -> None:
    23	        self.db.query(UserAllergy).filter(UserAllergy.user_id == user_id).delete()
    24	        for allergen_id in allergen_ids:
    25	            self.db.add(UserAllergy(user_id=user_id, allergen_id=allergen_id))
    26	        self.db.flush()

===== FILE: app/repositories/meal_record_repository.py =====
     1	from datetime import date, datetime
     2	
     3	from sqlalchemy import and_, select, update
     4	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session, joinedload
     5	
     6	from app.models.meal import Meal
     7	from app.models.meal_image import MealImage
     8	from app.models.meal_item_record import MealItemRecord
     9	from app.models.meal_menu_item import MealMenuItem
    10	from app.models.meal_record import MealRecord
    11	from app.models.menu import Menu
    12	from app.models.menu_allergen import MenuAllergen
    13	from app.models.menu_ingredient import MenuIngredient
    14	from app.utils.enums import MealRecordStatus
    15	
    16	
    17	class MealRecordRepository:
    18	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    19	        self.db = db
    20	
    21	    def _query(self):
    22	        return select(MealRecord).options(
    23	            joinedload(MealRecord.meal)
    24	            .joinedload(Meal.meal_menu_items)
    25	            .joinedload(MealMenuItem.menu)
    26	            .joinedload(Menu.ingredients)
    27	            .joinedload(MenuIngredient.ingredient),
    28	            joinedload(MealRecord.meal)
    29	            .joinedload(Meal.meal_menu_items)
    30	            .joinedload(MealMenuItem.menu)
    31	            .joinedload(Menu.allergens)
    32	            .joinedload(MenuAllergen.allergen),
    33	            joinedload(MealRecord.images),
    34	            joinedload(MealRecord.item_records)
    35	            .joinedload(MealItemRecord.meal_menu_item)
    36	            .joinedload(MealMenuItem.menu),
    37	        )
    38	
    39	    def create(self, *, user_id: int, meal_id: int) -> MealRecord:
    40	        record = MealRecord(user_id=user_id, meal_id=meal_id, status=MealRecordStatus.CREATED)
    41	        self.db.add(record)
    42	        self.db.flush()
    43	        return record
    44	
    45	    def get_by_id(self, meal_record_id: int) -> MealRecord | None:
    46	        stmt = self._query().where(MealRecord.id == meal_record_id)
    47	        return self.db.scalars(stmt).unique().one_or_none()
    48	
    49	    def get_by_user_and_meal(self, *, user_id: int, meal_id: int) -> MealRecord | None:
    50	        stmt = select(MealRecord).where(MealRecord.user_id == user_id, MealRecord.meal_id == meal_id)
    51	        return self.db.scalar(stmt)
    52	
    53	    def list_recent_completed_by_user(self, *, user_id: int, start_date: date, end_date: date) -> list[MealRecord]:
    54	        stmt = (
    55	            self._query()
    56	            .join(Meal, Meal.id == MealRecord.meal_id)
    57	            .where(
    58	                MealRecord.user_id == user_id,
    59	                MealRecord.status == MealRecordStatus.COMPLETED,
    60	                Meal.meal_date >= start_date,
    61	                Meal.meal_date <= end_date,
    62	            )
    63	            .order_by(Meal.meal_date.desc(), MealRecord.id.desc())
    64	        )
    65	        return list(self.db.scalars(stmt).unique().all())
    66	
    67	    def list_all(self) -> list[MealRecord]:
    68	        stmt = self._query().order_by(MealRecord.id.desc())
    69	        return list(self.db.scalars(stmt).unique().all())
    70	
    71	    def update_status(
    72	        self,
    73	        record: MealRecord,
    74	        *,
    75	        status: MealRecordStatus,
    76	        completed_at: datetime | None = None,
    77	        failure_reason: str | None = None,
    78	    ) -> MealRecord:
    79	        record.status = status
    80	        record.completed_at = completed_at
    81	        record.failure_reason = failure_reason
    82	        self.db.flush()
    83	        return record
    84	
    85	    def claim_for_analysis(self, meal_record_id: int, *, allowed_statuses: list[MealRecordStatus]) -> int:
    86	        stmt = (
    87	            update(MealRecord)
    88	            .where(MealRecord.id == meal_record_id, MealRecord.status.in_(allowed_statuses))
    89	            .values(status=MealRecordStatus.ANALYZING, completed_at=None, failure_reason=None)
    90	        )
    91	        result = self.db.execute(stmt)
    92	        return result.rowcount or 0

===== FILE: app/repositories/meal_item_record_repository.py =====
     1	from datetime import date
     2	
     3	from sqlalchemy import delete, select
     4	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session, joinedload
     5	
     6	from app.models.meal import Meal
     7	from app.models.meal_item_record import MealItemRecord
     8	from app.models.meal_menu_item import MealMenuItem
     9	from app.models.meal_record import MealRecord
    10	
    11	
    12	class MealItemRecordRepository:
    13	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    14	        self.db = db
    15	
    16	    def create_or_update(self, existing: MealItemRecord | None, **kwargs) -> MealItemRecord:
    17	        if existing:
    18	            for key, value in kwargs.items():
    19	                setattr(existing, key, value)
    20	            self.db.flush()
    21	            return existing
    22	        item = MealItemRecord(**kwargs)
    23	        self.db.add(item)
    24	        self.db.flush()
    25	        return item
    26	
    27	    def get_by_record_and_meal_menu_item(self, meal_record_id: int, meal_menu_item_id: int) -> MealItemRecord | None:
    28	        stmt = select(MealItemRecord).where(
    29	            MealItemRecord.meal_record_id == meal_record_id,
    30	            MealItemRecord.meal_menu_item_id == meal_menu_item_id,
    31	        )
    32	        return self.db.scalar(stmt)
    33	
    34	    def list_by_record(self, meal_record_id: int) -> list[MealItemRecord]:
    35	        stmt = (
    36	            select(MealItemRecord)
    37	            .options(joinedload(MealItemRecord.meal_menu_item).joinedload(MealMenuItem.menu))
    38	            .where(MealItemRecord.meal_record_id == meal_record_id)
    39	            .order_by(MealItemRecord.id.asc())
    40	        )
    41	        return list(self.db.scalars(stmt).all())
    42	
    43	    def get_by_id(self, meal_item_record_id: int) -> MealItemRecord | None:
    44	        stmt = (
    45	            select(MealItemRecord)
    46	            .options(
    47	                joinedload(MealItemRecord.meal_record).joinedload(MealRecord.meal),
    48	                joinedload(MealItemRecord.meal_menu_item).joinedload(MealMenuItem.menu),
    49	            )
    50	            .where(MealItemRecord.id == meal_item_record_id)
    51	        )
    52	        return self.db.scalars(stmt).unique().one_or_none()
    53	
    54	    def list_recent_same_menu_records(
    55	        self,
    56	        *,
    57	        user_id: int,
    58	        menu_id: int,
    59	        start_date: date,
    60	        end_date: date,
    61	        exclude_meal_id: int | None = None,
    62	    ) -> list[MealItemRecord]:
    63	        stmt = (
    64	            select(MealItemRecord)
    65	            .join(MealRecord, MealRecord.id == MealItemRecord.meal_record_id)
    66	            .join(Meal, Meal.id == MealRecord.meal_id)
    67	            .join(MealMenuItem, MealMenuItem.id == MealItemRecord.meal_menu_item_id)
    68	            .options(joinedload(MealItemRecord.meal_menu_item).joinedload(MealMenuItem.menu))
    69	            .where(
    70	                MealRecord.user_id == user_id,
    71	                Meal.meal_date >= start_date,
    72	                Meal.meal_date <= end_date,
    73	                MealMenuItem.menu_id == menu_id,
    74	                MealRecord.status == "COMPLETED",
    75	            )
    76	            .order_by(Meal.meal_date.desc(), MealItemRecord.id.desc())
    77	        )
    78	        if exclude_meal_id is not None:
    79	            stmt = stmt.where(MealRecord.meal_id != exclude_meal_id)
    80	        return list(self.db.scalars(stmt).all())
    81	
    82	    def delete_by_record(self, meal_record_id: int) -> None:
    83	        self.db.execute(delete(MealItemRecord).where(MealItemRecord.meal_record_id == meal_record_id))

===== FILE: app/repositories/meal_repository.py =====
     1	from datetime import date
     2	
     3	from sqlalchemy import select
     4	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session, joinedload
     5	
     6	from app.models.meal import Meal
     7	from app.models.meal_menu_item import MealMenuItem

     9	from app.models.menu_allergen import MenuAllergen
    10	from app.models.menu_ingredient import MenuIngredient
    11	from app.utils.datetime import get_current_date
    12	from app.utils.enums import MealType
    13	
    14	
    15	class MealRepository:
    16	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    17	        self.db = db
    18	
    19	    def _query(self):
    20	        return select(Meal).options(
    21	            joinedload(Meal.meal_menu_items)
    22	            .joinedload(MealMenuItem.menu)
    23	            .joinedload(Menu.ingredients)
    24	            .joinedload(MenuIngredient.ingredient),
    25	            joinedload(Meal.meal_menu_items)
    26	            .joinedload(MealMenuItem.menu)
    27	            .joinedload(Menu.allergens)
    28	            .joinedload(MenuAllergen.allergen),
    29	        )
    30	
    31	    def create(self, *, meal_date: date, meal_type: MealType, school_name: str) -> Meal:
    32	        meal = Meal(meal_date=meal_date, meal_type=meal_type, school_name=school_name)
    33	        self.db.add(meal)
    34	        self.db.flush()
    35	        return meal
    36	
    37	    def get_by_id(self, meal_id: int) -> Meal | None:
    38	        stmt = self._query().where(Meal.id == meal_id)
    39	        return self.db.scalars(stmt).unique().one_or_none()
    40	
    41	    def get_today(self, *, target_date: date | None = None, school_name: str | None = None) -> list[Meal]:
    42	        stmt = self._query().where(Meal.meal_date == (target_date or get_current_date()))
    43	        if school_name is not None:
    44	            stmt = stmt.where(Meal.school_name == school_name)
    45	        stmt = stmt.order_by(Meal.meal_type.asc())
    46	        return list(self.db.scalars(stmt).unique().all())
    47	
    48	    def get_today_meal_by_type(self, meal_type: MealType, *, target_date: date | None = None, school_name: str | None = None) -> Meal | None:
    49	        stmt = self._query().where(Meal.meal_date == (target_date or get_current_date()), Meal.meal_type == meal_type)
    50	        if school_name is not None:
    51	            stmt = stmt.where(Meal.school_name == school_name)
    52	        return self.db.scalars(stmt).unique().one_or_none()
    53	
    54	    def get_by_unique_fields(self, *, meal_date: date, meal_type: MealType, school_name: str) -> Meal | None:
    55	        stmt = select(Meal).where(Meal.meal_date == meal_date, Meal.meal_type == meal_type, Meal.school_name == school_name)
    56	        return self.db.scalar(stmt)

     1	from sqlalchemy import select
     2	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session, joinedload

     4	from app.models.allergen import Allergen

     6	from app.models.user_allergy import UserAllergy
     7	from app.models.user import User
     8	
     9	
    10	class RfidRepository:
    11	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    12	        self.db = db
    13	
    14	    def create(self, *, user_id: int, uid: str) -> RFIDCard:
    15	        card = RFIDCard(user_id=user_id, uid=uid, is_active=True)
    16	        self.db.add(card)
    17	        self.db.flush()
    18	        return card
    19	
    20	    def get_by_uid(self, uid: str) -> RFIDCard | None:
    21	        stmt = (
    22	            select(RFIDCard)
    23	            .options(joinedload(RFIDCard.user).joinedload(User.allergies).joinedload(UserAllergy.allergen))
    24	            .where(RFIDCard.uid == uid)
    25	        )
    26	        return self.db.scalar(stmt)
    27	
    28	    def get_active_by_uid(self, uid: str) -> RFIDCard | None:
    29	        stmt = (
    30	            select(RFIDCard)
    31	            .options(joinedload(RFIDCard.user).joinedload(User.allergies).joinedload(UserAllergy.allergen))
    32	            .join(User, User.id == RFIDCard.user_id)
    33	            .where(RFIDCard.uid == uid, RFIDCard.is_active.is_(True), User.is_active.is_(True))
    34	        )
    35	        return self.db.scalar(stmt)
    36	
    37	    def list_by_user(self, user_id: int) -> list[RFIDCard]:

    39	        return list(self.db.scalars(stmt).all())
    40	
    41	    def get_by_id(self, card_id: int) -> RFIDCard | None:
    42	        stmt = select(RFIDCard).where(RFIDCard.id == card_id)
    43	        return self.db.scalar(stmt)

===== FILE: app/core/exceptions.py =====
     1	from dataclasses import dataclass
     2	
     3	
     4	@dataclass
     5	class ErrorDetail:
     6	    code: str
     7	    detail: str | None = None
     8	
     9	
    10	class AppException(Exception):
    11	    def __init__(self, *, message: str, code: str, status_code: int, detail: str | None = None) -> None:
    12	        super().__init__(message)
    13	        self.message = message
    14	        self.code = code
    15	        self.status_code = status_code
    16	        self.detail = detail
    17	
    18	
    19	class BadRequestException(AppException):
    20	    def __init__(self, *, message: str, code: str, detail: str | None = None) -> None:
    21	        super().__init__(message=message, code=code, status_code=400, detail=detail)
    22	
    23	
    24	class UnauthorizedException(AppException):
    25	    def __init__(self, *, message: str, code: str, detail: str | None = None) -> None:
    26	        super().__init__(message=message, code=code, status_code=401, detail=detail)
    27	
    28	
    29	class ForbiddenException(AppException):
    30	    def __init__(self, *, message: str, code: str, detail: str | None = None) -> None:
    31	        super().__init__(message=message, code=code, status_code=403, detail=detail)
    32	
    33	
    34	class NotFoundException(AppException):
    35	    def __init__(self, *, message: str, code: str, detail: str | None = None) -> None:
    36	        super().__init__(message=message, code=code, status_code=404, detail=detail)
    37	
    38	
    39	class ConflictException(AppException):
    40	    def __init__(self, *, message: str, code: str, detail: str | None = None) -> None:
    41	        super().__init__(message=message, code=code, status_code=409, detail=detail)
    42	
    43	
    44	class ServerException(AppException):
    45	    def __init__(self, *, message: str, code: str, detail: str | None = None) -> None:
    46	        super().__init__(message=message, code=code, status_code=500, detail=detail)

     1	from app.services.storage.factory import build_image_storage

     7	
     8	def validate_storage_configuration() -> None:
     9	    build_image_storage().validate_configuration()

===== FILE: app/core/security.py =====
     1	from __future__ import annotations
     2	
     3	import base64
     4	import hashlib
     5	import hmac
     6	import json
     7	import secrets
     8	from datetime import UTC, datetime, timedelta
     9	
    10	from argon2 import PasswordHasher
    11	from argon2.exceptions import VerifyMismatchError
    12	from fastapi import Depends, Header
    13	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
    14	
    15	from app.core.config import settings
    16	from app.core.database import get_db
    17	from app.core.exceptions import ForbiddenException, UnauthorizedException
    18	from app.repositories.user_repository import UserRepository
    19	from app.utils.enums import UserRole
    20	
    21	password_hasher = PasswordHasher()
    22	
    23	
    24	def hash_password(password: str) -> str:
    25	    return password_hasher.hash(password)
    26	
    27	
    28	def verify_password(password: str, hashed_password: str) -> bool:
    29	    try:
    30	        return password_hasher.verify(hashed_password, password)
    31	    except VerifyMismatchError:
    32	        return False
    33	
    34	
    35	def _b64_encode(data: bytes) -> str:
    36	    return base64.urlsafe_b64encode(data).rstrip(b"=").decode("ascii")
    37	
    38	
    39	def _b64_decode(data: str) -> bytes:
    40	    return base64.urlsafe_b64decode(data + "=" * (-len(data) % 4))
    41	
    42	
    43	def _jwt_encode(payload: dict[str, object]) -> str:
    44	    header = {"alg": settings.JWT_ALGORITHM, "typ": "JWT"}
    45	    encoded_header = _b64_encode(json.dumps(header, separators=(",", ":")).encode("utf-8"))
    46	    encoded_payload = _b64_encode(json.dumps(payload, separators=(",", ":")).encode("utf-8"))
    47	    signing_input = f"{encoded_header}.{encoded_payload}".encode("ascii")
    48	    signature = hmac.new(settings.JWT_SECRET_KEY.encode("utf-8"), signing_input, hashlib.sha256).digest()
    49	    return f"{encoded_header}.{encoded_payload}.{_b64_encode(signature)}"
    50	
    51	
    52	def _jwt_decode(token: str) -> dict[str, object]:
    53	    try:
    54	        header, payload, signature = token.split(".")
    55	    except ValueError as exc:
    56	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="유효하지 않은 토큰입니다.", code="INVALID_TOKEN", detail="토큰 형식 오류") from exc
    57	
    58	    signing_input = f"{header}.{payload}".encode("ascii")
    59	    expected = hmac.new(settings.JWT_SECRET_KEY.encode("utf-8"), signing_input, hashlib.sha256).digest()
    60	    if not hmac.compare_digest(_b64_encode(expected), signature):
    61	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="유효하지 않은 토큰입니다.", code="INVALID_TOKEN", detail="토큰 서명 불일치")
    62	    try:
    63	        data = json.loads(_b64_decode(payload))
    64	    except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError) as exc:
    65	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="유효하지 않은 토큰입니다.", code="INVALID_TOKEN", detail="토큰 해석 실패") from exc
    66	    exp = data.get("exp")
    67	    if not isinstance(exp, int):
    68	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="유효하지 않은 토큰입니다.", code="INVALID_TOKEN", detail="만료 시각 누락")
    69	    if exp <= int(datetime.now(UTC).timestamp()):
    70	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="토큰이 만료되었습니다.", code="TOKEN_EXPIRED", detail="다시 로그인해 주세요.")
    71	    return data
    72	
    73	
    74	def create_access_token(user_id: int, role: UserRole | str) -> str:
    75	    now = datetime.now(UTC)
    76	    role_value = role.value if isinstance(role, UserRole) else str(role)
    77	    payload = {
    78	        "sub": str(user_id),
    79	        "role": role_value,
    80	        "type": "access",
    81	        "jti": secrets.token_urlsafe(16),
    82	        "iat": int(now.timestamp()),
    83	        "exp": int((now + timedelta(minutes=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)).timestamp()),
    84	    }
    85	    return _jwt_encode(payload)
    86	
    87	
    88	def create_refresh_token(user_id: int) -> tuple[str, datetime]:
    89	    now = datetime.now(UTC)
    90	    expires_at = now + timedelta(days=settings.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS)
    91	    payload = {
    92	        "sub": str(user_id),
    93	        "type": "refresh",
    94	        "jti": secrets.token_urlsafe(24),
    95	        "iat": int(now.timestamp()),
    96	        "exp": int(expires_at.timestamp()),
    97	    }
    98	    return _jwt_encode(payload), expires_at
    99	
   100	
   101	def decode_token(token: str) -> dict[str, object]:
   102	    return _jwt_decode(token)
   103	
   104	
   105	def hash_token(token: str) -> str:
   106	    return hashlib.sha256(token.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
   107	
   108	
   109	def validate_password_format(password: str) -> None:
   110	    has_upper = any(char.isupper() for char in password)
   111	    has_lower = any(char.islower() for char in password)
   112	    has_digit = any(char.isdigit() for char in password)
   113	    has_special = any(not char.isalnum() for char in password)
   114	    if len(password) < 8 or not (has_upper and has_lower and has_digit and has_special):
   115	        raise UnauthorizedException(
   116	            message="비밀번호 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.",
   117	            code="INVALID_PASSWORD_FORMAT",
   118	            detail="비밀번호는 8자 이상이며 대문자, 소문자, 숫자, 특수문자를 포함해야 합니다.",
   119	        )
   120	
   121	
   122	def _extract_bearer_token(authorization: str | None) -> str:
   123	    if not authorization:
   124	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="인증이 필요합니다.", code="INVALID_TOKEN", detail="Authorization 헤더가 필요합니다.")
   125	    scheme, _, token = authorization.partition(" ")
   126	    if scheme.lower() != "bearer" or not token:
   127	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="유효하지 않은 토큰입니다.", code="INVALID_TOKEN", detail="Bearer 토큰 형식 필요")
   128	    return token
   129	
   130	
   131	def get_current_user(authorization: str | None = Header(default=None, alias="Authorization"), db: Session = Depends(get_db)):
   132	    token = _extract_bearer_token(authorization)
   133	    payload = decode_token(token)
   134	    if payload.get("type") != "access":
   135	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="유효하지 않은 토큰입니다.", code="INVALID_TOKEN", detail="Access token만 허용됩니다.")
   136	    raw_user_id = payload.get("sub")
   137	    if not isinstance(raw_user_id, str) or not raw_user_id.isdigit():
   138	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="유효하지 않은 토큰입니다.", code="INVALID_TOKEN", detail="사용자 정보가 올바르지 않습니다.")
   139	    user = UserRepository(db).get_by_id(int(raw_user_id))
   140	    if not user:
   141	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="사용자를 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="USER_NOT_FOUND", detail=f"user_id={raw_user_id}")
   142	    if not user.is_active:
   143	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="비활성화된 계정입니다.", code="INACTIVE_USER", detail=f"user_id={user.id}")
   144	    return user
   145	
   146	
   147	def require_admin(current_user=Depends(get_current_user)):
   148	    if current_user.role != UserRole.ADMIN:
   149	        raise ForbiddenException(message="관리자 권한이 필요합니다.", code="ADMIN_REQUIRED", detail=f"user_id={current_user.id}")
   150	    return current_user
   151	
   152	
   153	def require_device_key(x_device_key: str | None = Header(default=None, alias="X-Device-Key")) -> str:
   154	    if not x_device_key or x_device_key != settings.DEVICE_API_KEY:
   155	        raise UnauthorizedException(message="장치 인증에 실패했습니다.", code="INVALID_DEVICE_KEY", detail="유효한 X-Device-Key 필요")
   156	    return x_device_key

===== FILE: app/core/database.py =====
     1	from collections.abc import Generator
     2	
     3	from sqlalchemy import create_engine, event
     4	from sqlalchemy.engine import Engine
     5	from sqlalchemy.orm import DeclarativeBase, Session, sessionmaker
     6	
     7	from app.core.config import settings
     8	
     9	
    10	class Base(DeclarativeBase):
    11	    pass
    12	
    13	
    14	engine = create_engine(
    15	    settings.DATABASE_URL,
    16	    connect_args={"check_same_thread": False} if settings.is_sqlite else {},
    17	    pool_pre_ping=not settings.is_sqlite,
    18	    pool_recycle=300 if settings.is_postgresql else -1,
    19	)
    20	
    21	
    22	@event.listens_for(Engine, "connect")
    23	def set_sqlite_pragma(dbapi_connection, connection_record):  # noqa: ANN001, ARG001
    24	    module_name = type(dbapi_connection).__module__
    25	    if "sqlite3" not in module_name:
    26	        return
    27	    cursor = dbapi_connection.cursor()
    28	    cursor.execute("PRAGMA foreign_keys=ON")
    29	    cursor.close()
    30	
    31	
    32	SessionLocal = sessionmaker(bind=engine, autoflush=False, autocommit=False, expire_on_commit=False, class_=Session)
    33	
    34	
    35	def get_db() -> Generator[Session, None, None]:
    36	    db = SessionLocal()
    37	    try:
    38	        yield db
    39	    finally:
    40	        db.close()

===== FILE: app/core/config.py =====
     1	import os
     2	from functools import lru_cache
     3	from pathlib import Path
     4	from zoneinfo import ZoneInfo
     5	
     6	from pydantic import Field, model_validator
     7	from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings, SettingsConfigDict
     8	
     9	
    10	class Settings(BaseSettings):
    11	    APP_NAME: str = "smart-meal-api"
    12	    APP_ENV: str = "development"
    13	    DEBUG: bool = True
    14	
    15	    DATABASE_URL: str = "sqlite:///./meal_service.db"
    16	    DATABASE_URL_UNPOOLED: str | None = None
    17	    SCHOOL_NAME: str = "국민대학교"
    18	    APP_TIMEZONE: str = "Asia/Seoul"
    19	
    20	    JWT_SECRET_KEY: str = "replace-with-secure-secret"
    21	    JWT_ALGORITHM: str = "HS256"
    22	    ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES: int = 60
    23	    REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS: int = 14
    24	
    25	    DEVICE_API_KEY: str = "replace-with-device-key"
    26	    PORT: int = 8000
    27	    RUN_MIGRATIONS_ON_START: bool = True
    28	
    29	    GEMINI_API_KEY: str | None = None
    30	    GEMINI_MODEL: str | None = None
    31	
    32	    OPENAI_API_KEY: str | None = None
    33	    OPENAI_MODEL: str | None = None
    34	    VISION_MODEL: str | None = None
    35	    VISION_ANALYSIS_MODE: str = "MOCK"
    36	    VISION_TIMEOUT_SECONDS: int = 60
    37	    VISION_MAX_RETRIES: int = 2
    38	
    39	    STORAGE_BACKEND: str = "LOCAL"
    40	    BLOB_STORE_ID: str | None = None
    41	    BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN: str | None = None
    42	    VERCEL_OIDC_TOKEN: str | None = None
    43	    UPLOAD_DIR: str = "uploads"
    44	    MAX_IMAGE_SIZE_MB: int = 4
    45	    ANALYSIS_IMAGE_MAX_DIMENSION: int = 1600
    46	    ANALYSIS_IMAGE_JPEG_QUALITY: int = 80
    47	    CORS_ORIGINS: list[str] = Field(default_factory=lambda: ["http://localhost:3000", "http://localhost:5173"])
    48	
    49	    model_config = SettingsConfigDict(
    50	        env_file=".env",
    51	        env_file_encoding="utf-8",
    52	        case_sensitive=True,
    53	        extra="ignore",
    54	    )
    55	
    56	    @property
    57	    def upload_path(self) -> Path:
    58	        return Path(self.UPLOAD_DIR)
    59	
    60	    @property
    61	    def timezone(self) -> ZoneInfo:
    62	        return ZoneInfo(self.APP_TIMEZONE)
    63	
    64	    @property
    65	    def is_sqlite(self) -> bool:
    66	        return self.DATABASE_URL.startswith("sqlite")
    67	
    68	    @property
    69	    def is_postgresql(self) -> bool:
    70	        return self.DATABASE_URL.startswith("postgresql+psycopg://")
    71	
    72	    @property
    73	    def resolved_openai_model(self) -> str | None:
    74	        return self.OPENAI_MODEL or self.VISION_MODEL
    75	
    76	    @property
    77	    def is_vercel_blob(self) -> bool:
    78	        return self.STORAGE_BACKEND == "VERCEL_BLOB"
    79	
    80	    @property
    81	    def is_vercel_runtime(self) -> bool:
    82	        return bool(os.getenv("VERCEL"))
    83	
    84	    @property
    85	    def has_blob_auth(self) -> bool:
    86	        return bool(self.BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN or os.getenv("BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN"))
    87	
    88	    @staticmethod
    89	    def normalize_database_url(value: str) -> str:
    90	        if not value:
    91	            return value
    92	        if value == "sqlite:///./smart_meal.db":
    93	            return "sqlite:///./meal_service.db"
    94	        if value.startswith("postgres://"):
    95	            return "postgresql+psycopg://" + value[len("postgres://") :]
    96	        if value.startswith("postgresql://") and not value.startswith("postgresql+psycopg://"):
    97	            return "postgresql+psycopg://" + value[len("postgresql://") :]
    98	        return value
    99	
   100	    @model_validator(mode="after")
   101	    def validate_runtime_settings(self):
   102	        self.DATABASE_URL = self.normalize_database_url(self.DATABASE_URL)
   103	        if self.DATABASE_URL_UNPOOLED:
   104	            self.DATABASE_URL_UNPOOLED = self.normalize_database_url(self.DATABASE_URL_UNPOOLED)
   105	        allowed_modes = {"MOCK", "GEMINI_VLM", "OPENAI_VLM"}
   106	        allowed_storage_backends = {"LOCAL", "VERCEL_BLOB"}
   107	        if self.VISION_ANALYSIS_MODE not in allowed_modes:
   108	            raise ValueError("VISION_ANALYSIS_MODE must be one of MOCK, GEMINI_VLM, OPENAI_VLM.")
   109	        if self.STORAGE_BACKEND not in allowed_storage_backends:
   110	            raise ValueError("STORAGE_BACKEND must be one of LOCAL, VERCEL_BLOB.")
   111	        if self.VISION_ANALYSIS_MODE == "GEMINI_VLM":
   112	            if not self.GEMINI_API_KEY:
   113	                raise ValueError("GEMINI_API_KEY is required when VISION_ANALYSIS_MODE=GEMINI_VLM.")
   114	            if not self.GEMINI_MODEL:
   115	                raise ValueError("GEMINI_MODEL is required when VISION_ANALYSIS_MODE=GEMINI_VLM.")
   116	        if self.VISION_ANALYSIS_MODE == "OPENAI_VLM":
   117	            if not self.OPENAI_API_KEY:
   118	                raise ValueError("OPENAI_API_KEY is required when VISION_ANALYSIS_MODE=OPENAI_VLM.")
   119	            if not self.resolved_openai_model:
   120	                raise ValueError("OPENAI_MODEL or legacy VISION_MODEL is required when VISION_ANALYSIS_MODE=OPENAI_VLM.")
   121	        if self.STORAGE_BACKEND == "VERCEL_BLOB":
   122	            if not self.has_blob_auth:
   123	                raise ValueError("BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN is required when STORAGE_BACKEND=VERCEL_BLOB.")
   124	        if self.APP_ENV != "development":
   125	            self.DEBUG = False
   126	            if self.JWT_SECRET_KEY == "replace-with-secure-secret":
   127	                raise ValueError("JWT_SECRET_KEY must be changed outside development.")
   128	            if self.DEVICE_API_KEY == "replace-with-device-key":
   129	                raise ValueError("DEVICE_API_KEY must be changed outside development.")
   130	            if self.JWT_SECRET_KEY == self.DEVICE_API_KEY:
   131	                raise ValueError("JWT_SECRET_KEY and DEVICE_API_KEY must be different.")
   132	            if len(self.JWT_SECRET_KEY) < 32:
   133	                raise ValueError("JWT_SECRET_KEY must be at least 32 characters outside development.")
   134	            if len(self.DEVICE_API_KEY) < 32:
   135	                raise ValueError("DEVICE_API_KEY must be at least 32 characters outside development.")
   136	            if self.CORS_ORIGINS and all(("localhost" in origin or "127.0.0.1" in origin) for origin in self.CORS_ORIGINS):
   137	                raise ValueError("CORS_ORIGINS must include a non-localhost origin outside development.")
   138	            if self.DATABASE_URL.startswith("sqlite"):
   139	                raise ValueError("SQLite DATABASE_URL is not allowed outside development.")
   140	            if self.is_vercel_runtime and self.STORAGE_BACKEND != "VERCEL_BLOB":
   141	                raise ValueError("STORAGE_BACKEND=VERCEL_BLOB is required on Vercel production runtime.")
   142	            if self.STORAGE_BACKEND == "VERCEL_BLOB" and self.RUN_MIGRATIONS_ON_START:
   143	                self.RUN_MIGRATIONS_ON_START = False
   144	        return self
   145	
   146	
   147	@lru_cache
   148	def get_settings() -> Settings:
   149	    return Settings()
   150	
   151	
   152	settings = get_settings()

     1	from __future__ import annotations
     2	
     3	from app.schemas.meal_analysis import VisionAnalysisResultSchema

     8	class VisionService:
     9	    def __init__(self) -> None:

    11	
    12	    def current_analysis_type(self) -> AnalysisType:
    13	        return self.provider.analysis_type
    14	
    15	    async def analyze(
    16	        self,
    17	        *,
    18	        before_image: bytes,
    19	        before_mime_type: str,
    20	        after_image: bytes,
    21	        after_mime_type: str,
    22	        menu_items: list[dict] | list[VisionMenuInput],

    27	            before_mime_type=before_mime_type,
    28	            after_image=after_image,
    29	            after_mime_type=after_mime_type,
    30	            menu_items=normalized_items,
    31	        )
    32	        return self.provider.analysis_type, result

===== FILE: app/services/auth_service.py =====
     1	from datetime import UTC, datetime
     2	
     3	from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
     4	
     5	from app.core.config import settings
     6	from app.core.exceptions import BadRequestException, ConflictException, UnauthorizedException
     7	from app.core.security import (
     8	    create_access_token,
     9	    create_refresh_token,
    10	    decode_token,
    11	    hash_password,
    12	    hash_token,
    13	    validate_password_format,
    14	    verify_password,
    15	)
    16	from app.repositories.allergen_repository import AllergenRepository
    17	from app.repositories.auth_repository import AuthRepository
    18	from app.repositories.user_repository import UserRepository
    19	from app.schemas.auth import (
    20	    ChangePasswordRequest,
    21	    LoginRequest,
    22	    LogoutRequest,
    23	    RefreshTokenRequest,
    24	    SignUpRequest,
    25	    TokenPairResponse,
    26	)
    27	from app.utils.normalization import normalize_allergen_codes
    28	from app.utils.enums import UserRole
    29	
    30	
    31	class AuthService:
    32	    def __init__(self, db: Session) -> None:
    33	        self.db = db
    34	        self.user_repository = UserRepository(db)
    35	        self.auth_repository = AuthRepository(db)
    36	        self.allergen_repository = AllergenRepository(db)
    37	
    38	    def signup(self, request: SignUpRequest):
    39	        if self.user_repository.get_by_login_id(request.login_id):
    40	            raise ConflictException(message="이미 사용 중인 로그인 ID입니다.", code="DUPLICATE_LOGIN_ID", detail=request.login_id)
    41	        if self.user_repository.get_by_student_number(request.student_number):
    42	            raise ConflictException(
    43	                message="이미 사용 중인 학번입니다.",
    44	                code="DUPLICATE_STUDENT_NUMBER",
    45	                detail=request.student_number,
    46	        )
    47	        validate_password_format(request.password)
    48	        allergen_codes = normalize_allergen_codes(request.allergen_codes)
    49	        allergens = self.allergen_repository.get_by_codes(allergen_codes)
    50	        if len(allergens) != len(allergen_codes):
    51	            raise BadRequestException(message="유효하지 않은 알레르기 코드가 있습니다.", code="INVALID_ALLERGEN_CODE", detail="allergen")
    52	        try:
    53	            user = self.user_repository.create(
    54	                login_id=request.login_id,
    55	                hashed_password=hash_password(request.password),
    56	                name=request.name,
    57	                student_number=request.student_number,
    58	                role=UserRole.STUDENT,
    59	                is_active=True,
    60	            )
    61	            self.allergen_repository.replace_user_allergies(user.id, [item.id for item in allergens])
    62	            self.db.commit()
    63	            self.db.refresh(user)
    64	            return user
    65	        except Exception:
    66	            self.db.rollback()
    67	            raise
    68	
    69	    def login(self, request: LoginRequest) -> TokenPairResponse:
    70	        user = self.user_repository.get_by_login_id(request.login_id)
    71	        if not user or not verify_password(request.password, user.hashed_password):
    72	            raise UnauthorizedException(message="로그인에 실패했습니다.", code="INVALID_CREDENTIALS", detail="아이디 또는 비밀번호 불일치")
    73	        if not user.is_active:
    74	            raise UnauthorizedException(message="비활성화된 계정입니다.", code="INACTIVE_USER", detail=f"user_id={user.id}")
    75	        access_token = create_access_token(user.id, user.role)
    76	        refresh_token, expires_at = create_refresh_token(user.id)
    77	        self.auth_repository.create_refresh_token(user_id=user.id, token_hash=hash_token(refresh_token), expires_at=expires_at)
    78	        self.db.commit()
    79	        return TokenPairResponse(
    80	            access_token=access_token,
    81	            refresh_token=refresh_token,
    82	            access_token_expires_in=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES * 60,
    83	            refresh_token_expires_in_days=settings.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS,
    84	        )
    85	
    86	    def refresh(self, request: RefreshTokenRequest) -> TokenPairResponse:
    87	        payload = decode_token(request.refresh_token)
    88	        if payload.get("type") != "refresh":
    89	            raise UnauthorizedException(message="유효하지 않은 토큰입니다.", code="INVALID_TOKEN", detail="refresh token 필요")
    90	        token_hash = hash_token(request.refresh_token)
    91	        refresh_token = self.auth_repository.get_refresh_token(token_hash)
    92	        if not refresh_token or refresh_token.revoked_at is not None:
    93	            raise UnauthorizedException(message="유효하지 않은 토큰입니다.", code="INVALID_TOKEN", detail="폐기된 refresh token")
    94	        expires_at = refresh_token.expires_at
    95	        if expires_at.tzinfo is None:
    96	            expires_at = expires_at.replace(tzinfo=UTC)
    97	        if expires_at <= datetime.now(UTC):
    98	            raise UnauthorizedException(message="토큰이 만료되었습니다.", code="TOKEN_EXPIRED", detail="refresh token 만료")
    99	        token_user_sub = payload.get("sub")
   100	        if not isinstance(token_user_sub, str) or token_user_sub != str(refresh_token.user_id):
   101	            raise UnauthorizedException(message="유효하지 않은 토큰입니다.", code="INVALID_TOKEN", detail="refresh token user mismatch")
   102	        user = self.user_repository.get_by_id(refresh_token.user_id)
   103	        if not user:
   104	            raise UnauthorizedException(message="사용자를 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="USER_NOT_FOUND", detail="refresh token user")
   105	        if not user.is_active:
   106	            raise UnauthorizedException(message="비활성화된 계정입니다.", code="INACTIVE_USER", detail=f"user_id={user.id}")
   107	        access_token = create_access_token(user.id, user.role)
   108	        new_refresh_token, expires_at = create_refresh_token(user.id)
   109	        self.auth_repository.revoke_refresh_token(refresh_token, datetime.now(UTC))
   110	        self.auth_repository.create_refresh_token(user_id=user.id, token_hash=hash_token(new_refresh_token), expires_at=expires_at)
   111	        self.db.commit()
   112	        return TokenPairResponse(
   113	            access_token=access_token,
   114	            refresh_token=new_refresh_token,
   115	            access_token_expires_in=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES * 60,
   116	            refresh_token_expires_in_days=settings.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS,
   117	        )
   118	
   119	    def logout(self, request: LogoutRequest) -> None:
   120	        refresh_token = self.auth_repository.get_refresh_token(hash_token(request.refresh_token))
   121	        if refresh_token and refresh_token.revoked_at is None:
   122	            self.auth_repository.revoke_refresh_token(refresh_token, datetime.now(UTC))
   123	            self.db.commit()
   124	
   125	    def change_password(self, user_id: int, request: ChangePasswordRequest) -> None:
   126	        user = self.user_repository.get_by_id(user_id)
   127	        if not user or not verify_password(request.current_password, user.hashed_password):
   128	            raise UnauthorizedException(message="비밀번호 변경에 실패했습니다.", code="INVALID_CREDENTIALS", detail="현재 비밀번호 불일치")
   129	        validate_password_format(request.new_password)
   130	        user.hashed_password = hash_password(request.new_password)
   131	        self.auth_repository.revoke_all_by_user_id(user_id, datetime.now(UTC))
   132	        self.db.commit()

===== FILE: app/services/storage/vercel_blob_storage.py =====
     1	from __future__ import annotations
     2	
     3	from typing import NoReturn
     4	
     5	from app.core.config import settings
     6	from app.core.exceptions import BadRequestException, NotFoundException, ServerException
     7	from app.services.storage.base import ImageStorage
     8	from app.utils.enums import ImageType
     9	
    10	try:
    11	    from vercel.blob import BlobClient
    12	    from vercel.blob.errors import (
    13	        BlobAccessError,
    14	        BlobNoTokenProvidedError,
    15	        BlobNotFoundError,
    16	        BlobRequestAbortedError,
    17	        BlobServiceNotAvailable,
    18	        BlobServiceRateLimited,
    19	        BlobStoreNotFoundError,
    20	        BlobStoreSuspendedError,
    21	    )
    22	except ImportError:  # pragma: no cover
    23	    BlobClient = None
    24	    BlobAccessError = BlobNoTokenProvidedError = BlobNotFoundError = None
    25	    BlobRequestAbortedError = BlobServiceNotAvailable = BlobServiceRateLimited = None
    26	    BlobStoreNotFoundError = BlobStoreSuspendedError = None
    27	
    28	
    29	class VercelBlobStorage(ImageStorage):
    30	    backend_name = "VERCEL_BLOB"
    31	
    32	    def __init__(self) -> None:
    33	        self.read_write_token = settings.BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN
    34	        self.oidc_token = settings.VERCEL_OIDC_TOKEN
    35	
    36	    def build_key(self, *, meal_record_id: int, image_type: ImageType, filename: str) -> str:
    37	        return f"meal-images/{meal_record_id}/{image_type.value.lower()}/{filename}"
    38	
    39	    def save(self, *, key: str, content: bytes, content_type: str) -> str:
    40	        self.validate_configuration()
    41	        self._put_blob(key=key, content=content, content_type=content_type)
    42	        return key
    43	
    44	    def read(self, key: str) -> bytes:
    45	        self.validate_configuration()
    46	        data = self._read_blob(key)
    47	        if data is None:
    48	            raise NotFoundException(message="이미지 파일을 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="IMAGE_FILE_NOT_FOUND", detail="blob missing")
    49	        return data
    50	
    51	    def delete(self, key: str) -> None:
    52	        self.validate_configuration()
    53	        self._delete_blob(key)
    54	
    55	    def exists(self, key: str) -> bool:
    56	        self.validate_configuration()
    57	        metadata = self._head_blob(key)
    58	        return metadata is not None
    59	
    60	    def ensure_ready(self) -> None:
    61	        self.validate_configuration()
    62	
    63	    def validate_configuration(self) -> None:
    64	        if BlobClient is None:
    65	            raise RuntimeError("Vercel Blob SDK is not installed. Install the 'vercel' package.")
    66	        if not self.read_write_token:
    67	            raise RuntimeError("BLOB_READ_WRITE_TOKEN is not configured.")
    68	
    69	    def _create_client(self):
    70	        self.validate_configuration()
    71	        return BlobClient(token=self.read_write_token)
    72	
    73	    def _sanitize_key(self, key: str) -> str:
    74	        raw_key = key.strip()
    75	        if not raw_key:
    76	            raise BadRequestException(message="잘못된 이미지 저장 경로입니다.", code="IMAGE_NOT_FOUND", detail="empty storage key")
    77	        if raw_key.startswith("/"):
    78	            raise BadRequestException(message="잘못된 이미지 저장 경로입니다.", code="IMAGE_NOT_FOUND", detail="absolute path is not allowed")
    79	        if raw_key.startswith(("http://", "https://")):
    80	            raise BadRequestException(message="잘못된 이미지 저장 경로입니다.", code="IMAGE_NOT_FOUND", detail="absolute url is not allowed")
    81	        if "\\" in raw_key:
    82	            raise BadRequestException(message="잘못된 이미지 저장 경로입니다.", code="IMAGE_NOT_FOUND", detail="backslash is not allowed")
    83	        parts = raw_key.split("/")
    84	        if any(part in {"", ".", ".."} for part in parts):
    85	            raise BadRequestException(message="잘못된 이미지 저장 경로입니다.", code="IMAGE_NOT_FOUND", detail="invalid path segments")
    86	        return raw_key
    87	
    88	    @staticmethod
    89	    def _get_status_code(exc: Exception) -> int | None:
    90	        status_code = getattr(exc, "status_code", None)
    91	        if isinstance(status_code, int):
    92	            return status_code
    93	        response = getattr(exc, "response", None)
    94	        response_status_code = getattr(response, "status_code", None)
    95	        if isinstance(response_status_code, int):
    96	            return response_status_code
    97	        return None
    98	
    99	    @staticmethod
   100	    def _is_not_found_error(exc: Exception) -> bool:
   101	        if BlobNotFoundError is not None and isinstance(exc, BlobNotFoundError):
   102	            return True
   103	        return VercelBlobStorage._get_status_code(exc) == 404
   104	
   105	    @staticmethod
   106	    def _raise_storage_error(exc: Exception, *, operation: str) -> NoReturn:
   107	        detail = f"{operation}:{type(exc).__name__}"
   108	        status_code = VercelBlobStorage._get_status_code(exc)
   109	        if BlobAccessError is not None and isinstance(exc, (BlobAccessError, BlobNoTokenProvidedError)):
   110	            raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소 인증에 실패했습니다.", code="STORAGE_AUTHENTICATION_FAILED", detail=detail) from exc
   111	        if BlobStoreNotFoundError is not None and isinstance(exc, BlobStoreNotFoundError):
   112	            raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소 설정이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="STORAGE_CONFIGURATION_ERROR", detail=detail) from exc
   113	        if BlobStoreSuspendedError is not None and isinstance(exc, BlobStoreSuspendedError):
   114	            raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="STORAGE_UNAVAILABLE", detail=detail) from exc
   115	        if BlobServiceNotAvailable is not None and isinstance(exc, BlobServiceNotAvailable):
   116	            raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="STORAGE_UNAVAILABLE", detail=detail) from exc
   117	        if BlobServiceRateLimited is not None and isinstance(exc, BlobServiceRateLimited):
   118	            raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="STORAGE_UNAVAILABLE", detail=detail) from exc
   119	        if BlobRequestAbortedError is not None and isinstance(exc, BlobRequestAbortedError):
   120	            raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="STORAGE_UNAVAILABLE", detail=detail) from exc
   121	        if status_code == 401:
   122	            raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소 인증에 실패했습니다.", code="STORAGE_AUTHENTICATION_FAILED", detail=detail) from exc
   123	        if status_code == 403:
   124	            raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소 권한이 없습니다.", code="STORAGE_PERMISSION_DENIED", detail=detail) from exc
   125	        if status_code == 400:
   126	            raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소 요청 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="STORAGE_REQUEST_INVALID", detail=detail) from exc
   127	        raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="STORAGE_UNAVAILABLE", detail=detail) from exc
   128	
   129	    def _put_blob(self, *, key: str, content: bytes, content_type: str) -> None:
   130	        normalized_key = self._sanitize_key(key)
   131	        try:
   132	            with self._create_client() as client:
   133	                result = client.put(
   134	                    normalized_key,
   135	                    content,
   136	                    access="private",
   137	                    content_type=content_type,
   138	                    add_random_suffix=False,
   139	                    overwrite=False,
   140	                )
   141	        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   142	            self._raise_storage_error(exc, operation="upload")
   143	        if result is None:
   144	            raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="STORAGE_UNAVAILABLE", detail="upload:empty_result")
   145	
   146	    def _read_blob(self, key: str) -> bytes | None:
   147	        normalized_key = self._sanitize_key(key)
   148	        try:
   149	            with self._create_client() as client:
   150	                content = client.get(normalized_key, access="private")
   151	        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   152	            if self._is_not_found_error(exc):
   153	                return None
   154	            self._raise_storage_error(exc, operation="read")
   155	        if content is None:
   156	            return None
   157	        if isinstance(content, bytes):
   158	            return content
   159	        payload = getattr(content, "content", None)
   160	        if isinstance(payload, bytes):
   161	            return payload
   162	        if hasattr(content, "read"):
   163	            return content.read()
   164	        raise ServerException(message="이미지 저장소를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="STORAGE_UNAVAILABLE", detail="read:unexpected_response_type")
   165	
   166	    def _head_blob(self, key: str):
   167	        normalized_key = self._sanitize_key(key)
   168	        try:
   169	            with self._create_client() as client:
   170	                return client.head(normalized_key)
   171	        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   172	            if self._is_not_found_error(exc):
   173	                return None
   174	            self._raise_storage_error(exc, operation="head")
   175	
   176	    def _delete_blob(self, key: str) -> None:
   177	        normalized_key = self._sanitize_key(key)
   178	        try:
   179	            with self._create_client() as client:
   180	                client.delete(normalized_key)
   181	        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   182	            if self._is_not_found_error(exc):
   183	                return
   184	            self._raise_storage_error(exc, operation="delete")

===== FILE: app/services/storage/base.py =====
     1	from __future__ import annotations
     2	
     3	from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
     4	from pathlib import Path
     5	
     6	from app.utils.enums import ImageType
     7	
     8	
     9	class ImageStorage(ABC):
    10	    backend_name: str
    11	
    12	    @abstractmethod
    13	    def build_key(self, *, meal_record_id: int, image_type: ImageType, filename: str) -> str:
    14	        ...
    15	
    16	    @abstractmethod
    17	    def save(self, *, key: str, content: bytes, content_type: str) -> str:
    18	        ...
    19	
    20	    @abstractmethod
    21	    def read(self, key: str) -> bytes:
    22	        ...
    23	
    24	    @abstractmethod
    25	    def delete(self, key: str) -> None:
    26	        ...
    27	
    28	    @abstractmethod
    29	    def exists(self, key: str) -> bool:
    30	        ...
    31	
    32	    @abstractmethod
    33	    def ensure_ready(self) -> None:
    34	        ...
    35	
    36	    @abstractmethod
    37	    def validate_configuration(self) -> None:
    38	        ...
    39	
    40	    def resolve_local_path(self, key: str) -> Path | None:
    41	        return None

===== FILE: app/services/storage/local_storage.py =====
     1	from __future__ import annotations
     2	
     3	import tempfile
     4	from pathlib import Path
     5	
     6	from app.core.config import settings
     7	from app.core.exceptions import BadRequestException, NotFoundException
     8	from app.services.storage.base import ImageStorage
     9	from app.utils.enums import ImageType
    10	
    11	
    12	class LocalImageStorage(ImageStorage):
    13	    backend_name = "LOCAL"
    14	
    15	    def build_key(self, *, meal_record_id: int, image_type: ImageType, filename: str) -> str:  # noqa: ARG002
    16	        return f"{image_type.value.lower()}/{filename}"
    17	
    18	    def save(self, *, key: str, content: bytes, content_type: str) -> str:  # noqa: ARG002
    19	        path = self.resolve_local_path(key)
    20	        if path is None:
    21	            raise RuntimeError("Local storage path resolution failed.")
    22	        path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    23	        path.write_bytes(content)
    24	        return key
    25	
    26	    def read(self, key: str) -> bytes:
    27	        path = self.resolve_local_path(key)
    28	        if path is None or not path.exists():
    29	            raise NotFoundException(message="이미지 파일을 찾을 수 없습니다.", code="IMAGE_FILE_NOT_FOUND", detail="storage key missing")
    30	        return path.read_bytes()
    31	
    32	    def delete(self, key: str) -> None:
    33	        path = self.resolve_local_path(key)
    34	        if path is not None and path.exists() and path.is_file():
    35	            path.unlink()
    36	
    37	    def exists(self, key: str) -> bool:
    38	        path = self.resolve_local_path(key)
    39	        return bool(path and path.exists())
    40	
    41	    def ensure_ready(self) -> None:
    42	        root = settings.upload_path
    43	        probe = None
    44	        try:
    45	            root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    46	            for child in ("before", "after"):
    47	                (root / child).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    48	            with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(dir=root, prefix=".write-test-", delete=False) as tmp:
    49	                tmp.write(b"ok")
    50	                probe = Path(tmp.name)
    51	            if probe is not None and probe.exists():
    52	                probe.unlink()
    53	        except OSError as exc:
    54	            if probe is not None and probe.exists():
    55	                probe.unlink()
    56	            raise RuntimeError("Upload storage is not writable.") from exc
    57	
    58	    def validate_configuration(self) -> None:
    59	        self.ensure_ready()
    60	
    61	    def resolve_local_path(self, key: str) -> Path | None:
    62	        safe_root = Path(settings.UPLOAD_DIR).resolve()
    63	        candidate = (safe_root / key).resolve()
    64	        if not str(candidate).startswith(str(safe_root)):
    65	            raise BadRequestException(message="잘못된 파일 경로입니다.", code="IMAGE_NOT_FOUND", detail="invalid storage path")
    66	        return candidate

===== FILE: app/utils/normalization.py =====
     1	def normalize_allergen_codes(codes: list[str] | None) -> list[str]:
     2	    if not codes:
     3	        return []
     4	    seen: set[str] = set()
     5	    normalized: list[str] = []
     6	    for code in codes:
     7	        item = code.strip().upper()
     8	        if not item or item in seen:
     9	            continue
    10	        seen.add(item)
    11	        normalized.append(item)
    12	    return normalized
    13	
    14	
    15	def normalize_ingredient_names(items: list[str] | None) -> list[str]:
    16	    if not items:
    17	        return []
    18	    seen: set[str] = set()
    19	    normalized: list[str] = []
    20	    for raw in items:
    21	        item = raw.strip()
    22	        if not item or item in seen:
    23	            continue
    24	        seen.add(item)
    25	        normalized.append(item)
    26	    return normalized

===== FILE: app/utils/files.py =====
     1	import base64
     2	import io
     3	import uuid
     4	from pathlib import Path
     5	
     6	from fastapi import UploadFile
     7	from PIL import Image, ImageOps, UnidentifiedImageError
     8	
     9	from app.core.config import settings
    10	from app.core.exceptions import BadRequestException
    11	
    12	ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS = {".jpg", ".jpeg", ".png", ".webp"}
    13	ALLOWED_MIME_TYPES = {"image/jpeg", "image/png", "image/webp"}
    14	FORMAT_BY_MIME = {"image/jpeg": "JPEG", "image/png": "PNG", "image/webp": "WEBP"}
    15	EXTENSION_BY_FORMAT = {"JPEG": ".jpg", "PNG": ".png", "WEBP": ".webp"}
    16	MIME_BY_FORMAT = {"JPEG": "image/jpeg", "PNG": "image/png", "WEBP": "image/webp"}
    17	
    18	
    19	def ensure_directory(path: Path) -> None:
    20	    path.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    21	
    22	
    23	def validate_extension(filename: str) -> str:
    24	    extension = Path(filename).suffix.lower()
    25	    if extension not in ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS:
    26	        raise BadRequestException(
    27	            message="지원하지 않는 이미지 형식입니다.",
    28	            code="INVALID_IMAGE_FORMAT",
    29	            detail=f"허용 확장자: {sorted(ALLOWED_EXTENSIONS)}",
    30	        )
    31	    return extension
    32	
    33	
    34	def validate_mime_type(mime_type: str | None) -> str:
    35	    if mime_type not in ALLOWED_MIME_TYPES:
    36	        raise BadRequestException(
    37	            message="지원하지 않는 이미지 형식입니다.",
    38	            code="INVALID_IMAGE_FORMAT",
    39	            detail=f"허용 MIME 타입: {sorted(ALLOWED_MIME_TYPES)}",
    40	        )
    41	    return str(mime_type)
    42	
    43	
    44	def validate_file_size(file_bytes: bytes) -> None:
    45	    max_size = settings.MAX_IMAGE_SIZE_MB * 1024 * 1024
    46	    if len(file_bytes) > max_size:
    47	        raise BadRequestException(
    48	            message="이미지 크기 제한을 초과했습니다.",
    49	            code="IMAGE_TOO_LARGE",
    50	            detail=f"최대 {settings.MAX_IMAGE_SIZE_MB}MB 허용",
    51	        )
    52	
    53	
    54	def generate_filename(original_filename: str) -> str:
    55	    return f"{uuid.uuid4().hex}{validate_extension(original_filename)}"
    56	
    57	
    58	def generate_filename_for_extension(extension: str) -> str:
    59	    return f"{uuid.uuid4().hex}{extension}"
    60	
    61	
    62	def save_image_bytes(*, file_bytes: bytes, filename: str, image_type: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
    63	    ensure_directory(Path(settings.UPLOAD_DIR) / image_type.lower())
    64	    target = Path(settings.UPLOAD_DIR) / image_type.lower() / filename
    65	    target.write_bytes(file_bytes)
    66	    return filename, str(target)
    67	
    68	
    69	def build_storage_path(image_type: str, filename: str) -> str:
    70	    return f"{image_type.lower()}/{filename}"
    71	
    72	
    73	def delete_file_if_exists(path_value: str | Path | None) -> None:
    74	    if not path_value:
    75	        return
    76	    path = Path(path_value)
    77	    if path.exists() and path.is_file():
    78	        path.unlink()
    79	
    80	
    81	def file_to_base64(path: str | Path) -> str:
    82	    return base64.b64encode(Path(path).read_bytes()).decode("ascii")
    83	
    84	
    85	def read_upload_file(upload_file: UploadFile) -> tuple[bytes, str, str]:
    86	    declared_mime_type = validate_mime_type(upload_file.content_type)
    87	    filename = upload_file.filename or "upload.jpg"
    88	    validate_extension(filename)
    89	    file_bytes = upload_file.file.read()
    90	    validate_file_size(file_bytes)
    91	    upload_file.file.seek(0)
    92	    try:
    93	        Image.open(io.BytesIO(file_bytes)).verify()
    94	        image = Image.open(io.BytesIO(file_bytes))
    95	    except (UnidentifiedImageError, OSError) as exc:
    96	        raise BadRequestException(message="유효하지 않은 이미지 파일입니다.", code="INVALID_IMAGE_FORMAT", detail="Pillow verification failed") from exc
    97	    image = ImageOps.exif_transpose(image)
    98	    image.load()
    99	    detected_format = (image.format or FORMAT_BY_MIME.get(declared_mime_type) or "").upper()
   100	    if detected_format not in EXTENSION_BY_FORMAT:
   101	        raise BadRequestException(message="지원하지 않는 이미지 형식입니다.", code="INVALID_IMAGE_FORMAT", detail=f"detected format={detected_format}")
   102	    max_dimension = max(image.size)
   103	    if max_dimension > settings.ANALYSIS_IMAGE_MAX_DIMENSION:
   104	        image.thumbnail((settings.ANALYSIS_IMAGE_MAX_DIMENSION, settings.ANALYSIS_IMAGE_MAX_DIMENSION))
   105	    output = io.BytesIO()
   106	    save_format = detected_format
   107	    save_kwargs = {}
   108	    if save_format == "JPEG":
   109	        image = image.convert("RGB")
   110	        save_kwargs["quality"] = settings.ANALYSIS_IMAGE_JPEG_QUALITY
   111	        save_kwargs["optimize"] = True
   112	    elif save_format == "WEBP":
   113	        save_kwargs["quality"] = settings.ANALYSIS_IMAGE_JPEG_QUALITY
   114	    image.save(output, format=save_format, **save_kwargs)
   115	    processed_bytes = output.getvalue()
   116	    validate_file_size(processed_bytes)
   117	    actual_mime_type = MIME_BY_FORMAT[save_format]
   118	    return processed_bytes, actual_mime_type, EXTENSION_BY_FORMAT[save_format]
   119	
   120	
   121	def resolve_storage_path(stored_path: str) -> Path:
   122	    safe_root = Path(settings.UPLOAD_DIR).resolve()
   123	    candidate = (safe_root / stored_path).resolve()
   124	    if not str(candidate).startswith(str(safe_root)):
   125	        raise BadRequestException(message="잘못된 파일 경로입니다.", code="IMAGE_NOT_FOUND", detail="invalid storage path")
   126	    return candidate

     1	from __future__ import annotations
     2	
     3	import asyncio
     4	import random
     5	from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
     6	
     7	from pydantic import BaseModel, ConfigDict
     8	
     9	from app.core.exceptions import AppException, ServerException
    10	from app.schemas.meal_analysis import VisionAnalysisResultSchema
    11	from app.utils.enums import AnalysisType
    12	
    13	
    14	class VisionMenuInput(BaseModel):
    15	    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid")
    16	
    17	    meal_menu_item_id: int
    18	    menu_id: int
    19	    menu_name: str
    20	
    21	
    22	class VisionProviderError(AppException):
    23	    pass
    24	
    25	
    26	class GeminiVisionError(VisionProviderError):
    27	    pass
    28	
    29	
    30	class OpenAIVisionError(VisionProviderError):
    31	    pass
    32	
    33	
    34	class VisionProvider(ABC):
    35	    analysis_type: AnalysisType
    36	    provider_name: str
    37	    model_name: str
    38	
    39	    @abstractmethod
    40	    async def analyze(
    41	        self,
    42	        *,
    43	        before_image: bytes,
    44	        before_mime_type: str,
    45	        after_image: bytes,
    46	        after_mime_type: str,
    47	        menu_items: list[VisionMenuInput],
    48	    ) -> VisionAnalysisResultSchema:
    49	        ...
    50	
    51	
    52	def build_instruction(menu_items: list[VisionMenuInput]) -> str:
    53	    return (
    54	        "당신은 학교 급식 식전·식후 이미지 분석기입니다.\n"
    55	        "첫 번째 이미지는 식전 이미지이고, 두 번째 이미지는 식후 이미지입니다.\n"
    56	        "제공된 메뉴만 분석하며 새로운 메뉴를 추측해 추가하지 마세요.\n"
    57	        "음식의 위치, 남은 양, 용기 상태를 비교해 각 메뉴의 섭취율을 추정하세요.\n"
    58	        "consumed_ratio는 먹은 비율입니다.\n"
    59	        "- 전부 남았으면 0.0\n"
    60	        "- 절반 먹었으면 약 0.5\n"
    61	        "- 전부 먹었으면 1.0\n"
    62	        "가려짐이나 구도 차이가 크면 confidence를 낮추세요.\n"
    63	        "모든 menu item을 정확히 한 번씩 반환하세요.\n"
    64	        "DB에 없는 ID를 만들지 마세요.\n"
    65	        "반드시 JSON schema에 맞춰 응답하세요.\n"
    66	        f"분석 대상 메뉴 목록: {[item.model_dump() for item in menu_items]}"
    67	    )
