    69	
    70	def build_result_schema() -> dict:
    71	    return {
    72	        "type": "object",
    73	        "properties": {
    74	            "items": {
    75	                "type": "array",
    76	                "minItems": 1,
    77	                "items": {
    78	                    "type": "object",
    79	                    "properties": {
    80	                        "meal_menu_item_id": {"type": "integer"},
    81	                        "menu_id": {"type": "integer"},
    82	                        "menu_name": {"type": "string"},
    83	                        "consumed_ratio": {"type": "number", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 1},
    84	                        "confidence": {"type": "number", "minimum": 0, "maximum": 1},
    85	                        "note": {"type": ["string", "null"]},
    86	                    },
    87	                    "required": ["meal_menu_item_id", "menu_id", "menu_name", "consumed_ratio", "confidence", "note"],
    88	                    "additionalProperties": False,
    89	                },
    90	            },
    91	            "analysis_note": {"type": "string"},
    92	        },
    93	        "required": ["items", "analysis_note"],
    94	        "additionalProperties": False,
    95	    }
    96	
    97	
    98	async def retry_with_backoff(coro_factory, *, retries: int, should_retry, on_retry) -> VisionAnalysisResultSchema:
    99	    max_attempts = max(retries, 0) + 1
   100	    last_exc: Exception | None = None
   101	    for attempt in range(max_attempts):
   102	        try:
   103	            return await coro_factory()
   104	        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001
   105	            last_exc = exc
   106	            if attempt == max_attempts - 1 or not should_retry(exc):
   107	                raise
   108	            await on_retry(exc, attempt + 1)
   109	            await asyncio.sleep((2**attempt) + random.uniform(0, 0.25))
   110	    if last_exc:
   111	        raise last_exc
   112	    raise ServerException(message="VLM API 호출에 실패했습니다.", code="VISION_PROVIDER_UNAVAILABLE", detail="unknown")

===== FILE: app/services/vision/gemini_provider.py =====
     1	from __future__ import annotations
     2	
     3	import asyncio
     4	import json
     5	import logging
     6	import time
     7	from uuid import uuid4
     8	
     9	from pydantic import ValidationError
    10	
    11	from app.core.config import settings
    12	from app.schemas.meal_analysis import VisionAnalysisResultSchema
    13	from app.services.vision.base import GeminiVisionError, VisionMenuInput, VisionProvider, build_instruction, build_result_schema, retry_with_backoff
    14	from app.utils.enums import AnalysisType
    15	
    16	logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    17	
    18	
    19	class GeminiVisionProvider(VisionProvider):
    20	    analysis_type = AnalysisType.GEMINI_VLM
    21	    provider_name = "gemini"
    22	    _client_cache: dict[tuple[str, str], object] = {}
    23	
    24	    def __init__(self) -> None:
    25	        self.model_name = settings.GEMINI_MODEL or ""
    26	        self.timeout_seconds = settings.VISION_TIMEOUT_SECONDS
    27	        cache_key = (settings.GEMINI_API_KEY or "", self.model_name)
    28	        if cache_key not in self._client_cache:
    29	            self._client_cache[cache_key] = self._create_client()
    30	        self.client = self._client_cache[cache_key]
    31	
    32	    @staticmethod
    33	    def _create_client():
    34	        if not settings.GEMINI_API_KEY:
    35	            raise GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 설정 오류입니다.", code="VISION_CONFIGURATION_ERROR", status_code=500, detail="GEMINI_API_KEY missing")
    36	        if not settings.GEMINI_MODEL:
    37	            raise GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 설정 오류입니다.", code="VISION_CONFIGURATION_ERROR", status_code=500, detail="GEMINI_MODEL missing")
    38	        from google import genai
    39	
    40	        return genai.Client(api_key=settings.GEMINI_API_KEY)
    41	
    42	    @staticmethod
    43	    def _get_status_code(exc: Exception) -> int | None:
    44	        code = getattr(exc, "code", None)
    45	        if isinstance(code, int):
    46	            return code
    47	        status_code = getattr(exc, "status_code", None)
    48	        if isinstance(status_code, int):
    49	            return status_code
    50	        return None
    51	
    52	    @classmethod
    53	    def _should_retry(cls, exc: Exception) -> bool:
    54	        if isinstance(exc, (TimeoutError, asyncio.TimeoutError, ConnectionError)):
    55	            return True
    56	        status_code = cls._get_status_code(exc)
    57	        if status_code in {408, 429, 500, 502, 503, 504}:
    58	            return True
    59	        name = type(exc).__name__.lower()
    60	        detail = str(exc).lower()
    61	        if status_code is None and ("timeout" in name or "timeout" in detail):
    62	            return True
    63	        if status_code is None and ("connection" in name or "connection" in detail):
    64	            return True
    65	        if status_code is None and ("quota" in detail or "rate limit" in detail):
    66	            return True
    67	        return False
    68	
    69	    @classmethod
    70	    def _error_summary(cls, exc: Exception) -> str:
    71	        status_code = cls._get_status_code(exc)
    72	        if isinstance(exc, (TimeoutError, asyncio.TimeoutError)) or status_code == 408:
    73	            return "request timed out"
    74	        if status_code == 400:
    75	            return "request invalid"
    76	        if status_code == 401:
    77	            return "authentication failed"
    78	        if status_code == 403:
    79	            return "permission denied"
    80	        if status_code == 404:
    81	            return "model not found"
    82	        if status_code == 429:
    83	            return "quota exceeded"
    84	        if status_code in {500, 502, 503, 504}:
    85	            return "provider unavailable"
    86	        if isinstance(exc, ConnectionError):
    87	            return "provider unavailable"
    88	        detail = str(exc).lower()
    89	        if "quota" in detail or "rate limit" in detail:
    90	            return "quota exceeded"
    91	        if "timeout" in detail:
    92	            return "request timed out"
    93	        if "connection" in detail:
    94	            return "provider unavailable"
    95	        return "provider error"
    96	
    97	    def _map_error(self, exc: Exception) -> GeminiVisionError:
    98	        if isinstance(exc, (json.JSONDecodeError, ValidationError)):
    99	            return GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 응답 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="INVALID_VLM_RESPONSE", status_code=400, detail="invalid structured response")
   100	        status_code = self._get_status_code(exc)
   101	        detail = str(exc).lower()
   102	        summary = self._error_summary(exc)
   103	        if status_code == 400:
   104	            return GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 요청 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="VISION_REQUEST_INVALID", status_code=400, detail=summary)
   105	        if status_code == 401:
   106	            return GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 인증에 실패했습니다.", code="VISION_AUTHENTICATION_FAILED", status_code=502, detail=summary)
   107	        if status_code == 403:
   108	            return GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 권한이 없습니다.", code="VISION_PERMISSION_DENIED", status_code=403, detail=summary)
   109	        if status_code == 404:
   110	            return GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 요청 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="VISION_REQUEST_INVALID", status_code=400, detail=summary)
   111	        if status_code == 429 or "quota" in detail or "rate limit" in detail:
   112	            return GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 요청 한도를 초과했습니다.", code="VISION_QUOTA_EXCEEDED", status_code=503, detail=summary)
   113	        if status_code in {500, 502, 503, 504}:
   114	            return GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 공급자를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="VISION_PROVIDER_UNAVAILABLE", status_code=503, detail=summary)
   115	        if isinstance(exc, (TimeoutError, asyncio.TimeoutError)) or status_code == 408 or "timeout" in type(exc).__name__.lower() or "timeout" in detail:
   116	            return GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 요청 시간이 초과되었습니다.", code="VISION_TIMEOUT", status_code=503, detail=summary)
   117	        if isinstance(exc, ConnectionError) or "connection" in type(exc).__name__.lower() or "connection" in detail:
   118	            return GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 공급자에 연결할 수 없습니다.", code="VISION_PROVIDER_UNAVAILABLE", status_code=503, detail=summary)
   119	        return GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 공급자를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="VISION_PROVIDER_UNAVAILABLE", status_code=503, detail=summary)
   120	
   121	    async def analyze(
   122	        self,
   123	        *,
   124	        before_image: bytes,
   125	        before_mime_type: str,
   126	        after_image: bytes,
   127	        after_mime_type: str,
   128	        menu_items: list[VisionMenuInput],
   129	    ) -> VisionAnalysisResultSchema:
   130	        request_id = uuid4().hex
   131	        start_time = time.perf_counter()
   132	        try:
   133	            async def _call():
   134	                response = await asyncio.wait_for(
   135	                    self._generate_content(
   136	                        before_image=before_image,
   137	                        before_mime_type=before_mime_type,
   138	                        after_image=after_image,
   139	                        after_mime_type=after_mime_type,
   140	                        menu_items=menu_items,
   141	                    ),
   142	                    timeout=getattr(self, "timeout_seconds", settings.VISION_TIMEOUT_SECONDS),
   143	                )
   144	                return self._parse_response(response)
   145	
   146	            async def _on_retry(exc: Exception, attempt: int):
   147	                logger.warning(
   148	                    "vlm_retry provider=%s request_id=%s model=%s attempt=%s status_code=%s error=%s",
   149	                    self.provider_name,
   150	                    request_id,
   151	                    self.model_name,
   152	                    attempt,
   153	                    self._get_status_code(exc),
   154	                    self._error_summary(exc),
   155	                )
   156	
   157	            result = await retry_with_backoff(_call, retries=settings.VISION_MAX_RETRIES, should_retry=self._should_retry, on_retry=_on_retry)
   158	            logger.info(
   159	                "vlm_success provider=%s request_id=%s model=%s meal_menu_items=%s elapsed_ms=%s",
   160	                self.provider_name,
   161	                request_id,
   162	                self.model_name,
   163	                len(menu_items),
   164	                round((time.perf_counter() - start_time) * 1000, 2),
   165	            )
   166	            return result
   167	        except GeminiVisionError:
   168	            raise
   169	        except Exception as exc:
   170	            raise self._map_error(exc) from exc
   171	
   172	    async def _generate_content(
   173	        self,
   174	        *,
   175	        before_image: bytes,
   176	        before_mime_type: str,
   177	        after_image: bytes,
   178	        after_mime_type: str,
   179	        menu_items: list[VisionMenuInput],
   180	    ):
   181	        from google.genai import types
   182	
   183	        contents = [
   184	            types.Content(
   185	                role="user",
   186	                parts=[
   187	                    types.Part.from_text(text="첫 번째 이미지는 식전 이미지입니다."),
   188	                    types.Part.from_bytes(data=before_image, mime_type=before_mime_type),
   189	                    types.Part.from_text(text="두 번째 이미지는 식후 이미지입니다."),
   190	                    types.Part.from_bytes(data=after_image, mime_type=after_mime_type),
   191	                    types.Part.from_text(text=build_instruction(menu_items)),
   192	                ],
   193	            )
   194	        ]
   195	        config = types.GenerateContentConfig(
   196	            response_mime_type="application/json",
   197	            response_json_schema=build_result_schema(),
   198	            temperature=0,
   199	        )
   200	        return await self.client.aio.models.generate_content(model=self.model_name, contents=contents, config=config)
   201	
   202	    @staticmethod
   203	    def _parse_response(response) -> VisionAnalysisResultSchema:
   204	        output_text = getattr(response, "text", None)
   205	        if not output_text:
   206	            output_text = getattr(response, "output_text", None)
   207	        if not output_text:
   208	            raise GeminiVisionError(message="VLM 응답 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="INVALID_VLM_RESPONSE", status_code=400, detail="empty structured response")
   209	        return VisionAnalysisResultSchema.model_validate_json(output_text)

===== FILE: app/services/vision/openai_provider.py =====
     1	from __future__ import annotations
     2	
     3	import base64
     4	import json
     5	import logging
     6	import time
     7	from uuid import uuid4
     8	
     9	from pydantic import ValidationError
    10	
    11	from app.core.config import settings
    12	from app.schemas.meal_analysis import VisionAnalysisResultSchema
    13	from app.services.vision.base import OpenAIVisionError, VisionMenuInput, VisionProvider, build_instruction, build_result_schema, retry_with_backoff
    14	from app.utils.enums import AnalysisType
    15	
    16	logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
    17	
    18	
    19	class OpenAIVisionProvider(VisionProvider):
    20	    analysis_type = AnalysisType.OPENAI_VLM
    21	    provider_name = "openai"
    22	    _client_cache: dict[tuple[str, str], object] = {}
    23	
    24	    def __init__(self) -> None:
    25	        self.model_name = settings.resolved_openai_model or ""
    26	        cache_key = (settings.OPENAI_API_KEY or "", self.model_name)
    27	        if cache_key not in self._client_cache:
    28	            self._client_cache[cache_key] = self._create_client()
    29	        self.client = self._client_cache[cache_key]
    30	
    31	    @staticmethod
    32	    def _create_client():
    33	        from openai import AsyncOpenAI
    34	
    35	        if not settings.OPENAI_API_KEY:
    36	            raise OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 설정 오류입니다.", code="VISION_CONFIGURATION_ERROR", status_code=500, detail="OPENAI_API_KEY missing")
    37	        if not settings.resolved_openai_model:
    38	            raise OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 설정 오류입니다.", code="VISION_CONFIGURATION_ERROR", status_code=500, detail="OPENAI_MODEL missing")
    39	        return AsyncOpenAI(api_key=settings.OPENAI_API_KEY, timeout=settings.VISION_TIMEOUT_SECONDS)
    40	
    41	    @staticmethod
    42	    def _should_retry(exc: Exception) -> bool:
    43	        from openai import APIConnectionError, APIStatusError, APITimeoutError, RateLimitError
    44	
    45	        if isinstance(exc, (APITimeoutError, APIConnectionError, RateLimitError)):
    46	            return True
    47	        if isinstance(exc, APIStatusError):
    48	            status_code = getattr(exc, "status_code", None)
    49	            return status_code is not None and 500 <= status_code <= 599
    50	        return False
    51	
    52	    def _map_error(self, exc: Exception) -> OpenAIVisionError:
    53	        from openai import APIConnectionError, APIStatusError, APITimeoutError, AuthenticationError, BadRequestError, OpenAIError, PermissionDeniedError, RateLimitError
    54	
    55	        if isinstance(exc, AuthenticationError):
    56	            return OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 인증에 실패했습니다.", code="VISION_AUTHENTICATION_FAILED", status_code=401, detail="openai authentication failed")
    57	        if isinstance(exc, PermissionDeniedError):
    58	            return OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 권한이 없습니다.", code="VISION_PERMISSION_DENIED", status_code=403, detail="openai permission denied")
    59	        if isinstance(exc, BadRequestError):
    60	            return OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 요청 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="VISION_REQUEST_INVALID", status_code=400, detail="openai bad request")
    61	        if isinstance(exc, APITimeoutError):
    62	            return OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 요청 시간이 초과되었습니다.", code="VISION_TIMEOUT", status_code=503, detail="openai timeout")
    63	        if isinstance(exc, RateLimitError):
    64	            return OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 요청 한도를 초과했습니다.", code="VISION_QUOTA_EXCEEDED", status_code=503, detail="openai rate limit")
    65	        if isinstance(exc, APIConnectionError):
    66	            return OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 공급자에 연결할 수 없습니다.", code="VISION_PROVIDER_UNAVAILABLE", status_code=503, detail="openai connection error")
    67	        if isinstance(exc, APIStatusError):
    68	            status_code = getattr(exc, "status_code", None)
    69	            if status_code is not None and 500 <= status_code <= 599:
    70	                return OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 공급자를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="VISION_PROVIDER_UNAVAILABLE", status_code=503, detail=f"openai server status={status_code}")
    71	            return OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 요청에 실패했습니다.", code="VISION_REQUEST_INVALID", status_code=400, detail=f"openai status={status_code}")
    72	        if isinstance(exc, (json.JSONDecodeError, ValidationError)):
    73	            return OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 응답 형식이 올바르지 않습니다.", code="INVALID_VLM_RESPONSE", status_code=400, detail="invalid structured response")
    74	        if isinstance(exc, OpenAIError):
    75	            return OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 공급자를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="VISION_PROVIDER_UNAVAILABLE", status_code=503, detail="openai error")
    76	        return OpenAIVisionError(message="VLM 공급자를 사용할 수 없습니다.", code="VISION_PROVIDER_UNAVAILABLE", status_code=503, detail=type(exc).__name__)
    77	
    78	    async def analyze(
    79	        self,
    80	        *,
    81	        before_image: bytes,
    82	        before_mime_type: str,
    83	        after_image: bytes,
    84	        after_mime_type: str,
    85	        menu_items: list[VisionMenuInput],
    86	    ) -> VisionAnalysisResultSchema:
    87	        request_id = uuid4().hex
    88	        start_time = time.perf_counter()
    89	        prompt = {
    90	            "role": "user",
    91	            "content": [
    92	                {"type": "input_text", "text": build_instruction(menu_items)},
    93	                {"type": "input_image", "image_url": f"data:{before_mime_type};base64,{self._image_to_base64(before_image)}"},
    94	                {"type": "input_image", "image_url": f"data:{after_mime_type};base64,{self._image_to_base64(after_image)}"},
    95	            ],
    96	        }
    97	        try:
    98	            async def _call():
    99	                response = await self.client.responses.create(
   100	                    model=self.model_name,
   101	                    input=[prompt],
   102	                    text={
   103	                        "format": {
   104	                            "type": "json_schema",
   105	                            "name": "meal_analysis_result",
   106	                            "schema": build_result_schema(),
   107	                            "strict": True,
   108	                        }
   109	                    },
   110	                )
   111	                return VisionAnalysisResultSchema.model_validate_json(response.output_text)
   112	
   113	            async def _on_retry(exc: Exception, attempt: int):
   114	                logger.warning("vlm_retry provider=%s request_id=%s model=%s attempt=%s error=%s", self.provider_name, request_id, self.model_name, attempt, type(exc).__name__)
   115	
   116	            result = await retry_with_backoff(_call, retries=settings.VISION_MAX_RETRIES, should_retry=self._should_retry, on_retry=_on_retry)
   117	            logger.info(
   118	                "vlm_success provider=%s request_id=%s model=%s meal_menu_items=%s elapsed_ms=%s",
   119	                self.provider_name,
   120	                request_id,
   121	                self.model_name,
   122	                len(menu_items),
   123	                round((time.perf_counter() - start_time) * 1000, 2),
   124	            )
   125	            return result
   126	        except OpenAIVisionError:
   127	            raise
   128	        except Exception as exc:
   129	            raise self._map_error(exc) from exc
   130	
   131	    @staticmethod
   132	    def _image_to_base64(image_bytes: bytes) -> str:
   133	        return base64.b64encode(image_bytes).decode("ascii")

===== FILE: app/services/vision/factory.py =====
     1	from __future__ import annotations
     2	
     3	from app.core.config import settings
     4	from app.services.vision.base import VisionProvider
     5	from app.services.vision.gemini_provider import GeminiVisionProvider
     6	from app.services.vision.mock_provider import MockVisionProvider
     7	from app.services.vision.openai_provider import OpenAIVisionProvider
     8	from app.utils.enums import AnalysisType
     9	
    10	
    11	def build_vision_provider() -> VisionProvider:
    12	    analysis_type = AnalysisType(settings.VISION_ANALYSIS_MODE)
    13	    if analysis_type == AnalysisType.MOCK:
    14	        return MockVisionProvider()
    15	    if analysis_type == AnalysisType.GEMINI_VLM:
    16	        return GeminiVisionProvider()
    17	    if analysis_type == AnalysisType.OPENAI_VLM:
    18	        return OpenAIVisionProvider()
    19	    raise ValueError(f"Unsupported vision analysis mode: {settings.VISION_ANALYSIS_MODE}")

    13	    async def analyze(
    14	        self,

     9	class ServingRecommendation(TimestampedModel, Base):
    10	    __tablename__ = "serving_recommendations"
    11	    __table_args__ = (
    12	        UniqueConstraint("user_id", "meal_id", "meal_menu_item_id", name="uq_serving_recommendation_user_meal_item"),
    13	        CheckConstraint("recommended_serving_ratio > 0", name="ck_serving_recommendations_ratio_positive"),
    14	        CheckConstraint("recommended_serving_g >= 0", name="ck_serving_recommendations_serving_g_nonnegative"),
    15	        CheckConstraint(
    16	            "recent_average_consumed_ratio IS NULL OR (recent_average_consumed_ratio >= 0 AND recent_average_consumed_ratio <= 1)",
    17	            name="ck_serving_recommendations_recent_avg_range",
    18	        ),
    19	        CheckConstraint("sample_count >= 0", name="ck_serving_recommendations_sample_count_nonnegative"),
    20	    )
    21	
    22	    user_id: Mapped[int] = mapped_column(ForeignKey("users.id", ondelete="CASCADE"), nullable=False, index=True)
    23	    meal_id: Mapped[int] = mapped_column(ForeignKey("meals.id", ondelete="CASCADE"), nullable=False, index=True)
    24	    meal_menu_item_id: Mapped[int] = mapped_column(
    25	        ForeignKey("meal_menu_items.id", ondelete="CASCADE"),
    26	        nullable=False,
    27	        index=True,
    28	    )
    29	    recommendation_level: Mapped[RecommendationLevel] = mapped_column(String(20), nullable=False)
    30	    recommended_serving_ratio: Mapped[float] = mapped_column(Float, nullable=False)
    31	    recommended_serving_g: Mapped[float] = mapped_column(Float, nullable=False)
    32	    recent_average_consumed_ratio: Mapped[float | None] = mapped_column(Float, nullable=True)
    33	    sample_count: Mapped[int] = mapped_column(Integer, nullable=False, default=0)
    34	    reason: Mapped[str] = mapped_column(String(255), nullable=False)
    35	
    36	    user = relationship("User", back_populates="recommendations")
    37	    meal_menu_item = relationship("MealMenuItem", back_populates="recommendations")

===== FILE: app/models/base.py =====
     1	from datetime import datetime
     2	
     3	from sqlalchemy import BigInteger, DateTime, Integer, func
     4	from sqlalchemy.orm import Mapped, mapped_column
     5	
     6	
     7	BIGINT_PK = BigInteger().with_variant(Integer, "sqlite")
     8	
     9	
    10	class TimestampedModel:
    11	    id: Mapped[int] = mapped_column(BIGINT_PK, primary_key=True, autoincrement=True)
    12	    created_at: Mapped[datetime] = mapped_column(DateTime(timezone=True), server_default=func.now(), nullable=False)
    13	    updated_at: Mapped[datetime] = mapped_column(
    14	        DateTime(timezone=True),
    15	        server_default=func.now(),
    16	        onupdate=func.now(),
    17	        nullable=False,
    18	    )

===== FILE: app/models/rfid_card.py =====
     1	from datetime import datetime
     2	from typing import TYPE_CHECKING
     3	
     4	from sqlalchemy import Boolean, DateTime, ForeignKey, String, func
     5	from sqlalchemy.orm import Mapped, mapped_column, relationship

     1	from typing import TYPE_CHECKING
     2	
     3	from sqlalchemy import Boolean, CheckConstraint, Float, String
     4	from sqlalchemy.orm import Mapped, mapped_column, relationship
     5	
     6	from app.core.database import Base
     7	from app.models.base import TimestampedModel
     8	
     9	if TYPE_CHECKING:
    10	    from app.models.meal_menu_item import MealMenuItem
    11	    from app.models.menu_allergen import MenuAllergen
    12	    from app.models.menu_ingredient import MenuIngredient
    13	
    14	
    15	class Menu(TimestampedModel, Base):
    16	    __tablename__ = "menus"
    17	    __table_args__ = (
    18	        CheckConstraint("standard_serving_g > 0", name="ck_menus_standard_serving_g_positive"),
    19	        CheckConstraint("calories_per_100g >= 0", name="ck_menus_calories_nonnegative"),
    20	        CheckConstraint("carbohydrate_per_100g >= 0", name="ck_menus_carbohydrate_nonnegative"),
    21	        CheckConstraint("protein_per_100g >= 0", name="ck_menus_protein_nonnegative"),
    22	        CheckConstraint("fat_per_100g >= 0", name="ck_menus_fat_nonnegative"),
    23	    )
    24	
    25	    name: Mapped[str] = mapped_column(String(100), unique=True, index=True, nullable=False)
    26	    standard_serving_g: Mapped[float] = mapped_column(Float, nullable=False)
    27	    calories_per_100g: Mapped[float] = mapped_column(Float, nullable=False)
    28	    carbohydrate_per_100g: Mapped[float] = mapped_column(Float, nullable=False)
    29	    protein_per_100g: Mapped[float] = mapped_column(Float, nullable=False)
    30	    fat_per_100g: Mapped[float] = mapped_column(Float, nullable=False)
    31	    is_active: Mapped[bool] = mapped_column(Boolean, nullable=False, default=True)
    32	
    33	    ingredients: Mapped[list["MenuIngredient"]] = relationship(back_populates="menu", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
    34	    allergens: Mapped[list["MenuAllergen"]] = relationship(back_populates="menu", cascade="all, delete-orphan")
    35	    meal_menu_items: Mapped[list["MealMenuItem"]] = relationship(back_populates="menu")

===== FILE: app/api/mappers/response_mappers.py =====
     1	from app.schemas.admin import AdminDashboardResponse, LeftoverSummaryItemResponse
     2	from app.schemas.meal import MealDetailResponse, MealMenuItemResponse, NutritionPer100gSchema
     3	from app.schemas.meal_analysis import MealAnalysisResponse
     4	from app.schemas.meal_image import MealImageResponse
     5	from app.schemas.meal_record import MealItemRecordResponse, MealRecordDetailResponse
     6	from app.schemas.recommendation import RecommendationItemResponse
     7	from app.schemas.rfid import DeviceMealResponse, DeviceMenuGuidanceResponse, DeviceRfidScanResponse, DeviceUserResponse
     8	
     9	
    10	def to_meal_response(meal) -> MealDetailResponse:
    11	    return MealDetailResponse(
    12	        id=meal.id,
    13	        meal_date=meal.meal_date,
    14	        meal_type=meal.meal_type,
    15	        school_name=meal.school_name,
    16	        created_at=meal.created_at,
    17	        updated_at=meal.updated_at,
    18	        menu_items=[
    19	            MealMenuItemResponse(
    20	                meal_menu_item_id=item.id,
    21	                menu_id=item.menu_id,
    22	                name=item.menu.name,
    23	                standard_serving_g=item.menu.standard_serving_g,
    24	                nutrition_per_100g=NutritionPer100gSchema(
    25	                    calories_kcal=item.menu.calories_per_100g,
    26	                    carbohydrate_g=item.menu.carbohydrate_per_100g,
    27	                    protein_g=item.menu.protein_per_100g,
    28	                    fat_g=item.menu.fat_per_100g,
    29	                ),
    30	                ingredients=[link.ingredient.name for link in item.menu.ingredients],
    31	                allergens=[link.allergen.code for link in item.menu.allergens],
    32	            )
    33	            for item in meal.meal_menu_items
    34	        ],
    35	    )
    36	
    37	
    38	def to_meal_image_response(image) -> MealImageResponse:
    39	    return MealImageResponse(
    40	        id=image.id,
    41	        meal_record_id=image.meal_record_id,
    42	        image_type=image.image_type,
    43	        image_url=f"/api/v1/me/meal-images/{image.id}",
    44	        mime_type=image.mime_type,
    45	        file_size=image.file_size,
    46	        created_at=image.created_at,
    47	    )
    48	
    49	
    50	def to_meal_item_record_response(item, nutrition_service) -> MealItemRecordResponse:
    51	    return MealItemRecordResponse(
    52	        id=item.id,
    53	        meal_record_id=item.meal_record_id,
    54	        meal_menu_item_id=item.meal_menu_item_id,
    55	        menu_id=item.meal_menu_item.menu_id,
    56	        menu_name=item.meal_menu_item.menu.name,
    57	        consumed_ratio=item.consumed_ratio,
    58	        consumed_percent=round(item.consumed_ratio * 100, 2),
    59	        consumption_level=item.consumption_level,
    60	        confidence=item.confidence,
    61	        is_corrected=item.is_corrected,
    62	        corrected_at=item.corrected_at,
    63	        corrected_by=item.corrected_by,
    64	        note=item.note,
    65	        analysis_type=item.analysis_type.value if hasattr(item.analysis_type, "value") else str(item.analysis_type),
    66	        nutrition=nutrition_service.calculate(item.meal_menu_item.menu, item.consumed_ratio),
    67	        created_at=item.created_at,
    68	        updated_at=item.updated_at,
    69	    )
    70	
    71	
    72	def to_meal_record_response(record, nutrition_service) -> MealRecordDetailResponse:
    73	    return MealRecordDetailResponse(
    74	        id=record.id,
    75	        user_id=record.user_id,
    76	        meal_id=record.meal_id,
    77	        status=record.status,
    78	        started_at=record.started_at,
    79	        completed_at=record.completed_at,
    80	        failure_reason=record.failure_reason,
    81	        created_at=record.created_at,
    82	        updated_at=record.updated_at,
    83	        meal=to_meal_response(record.meal),
    84	        images=[to_meal_image_response(image) for image in record.images],
    85	        item_records=[to_meal_item_record_response(item, nutrition_service) for item in record.item_records],
    86	    )
    87	
    88	
    89	def to_recommendation_response(item) -> RecommendationItemResponse:
    90	    return RecommendationItemResponse(
    91	        meal_id=item.meal_id,
    92	        meal_menu_item_id=item.meal_menu_item_id,
    93	        menu_id=item.meal_menu_item.menu_id,
    94	        menu_name=item.meal_menu_item.menu.name,
    95	        standard_serving_g=item.meal_menu_item.menu.standard_serving_g,
    96	        recommendation_level=item.recommendation_level,
    97	        recommended_serving_ratio=item.recommended_serving_ratio,
    98	        recommended_serving_g=item.recommended_serving_g,
    99	        recent_average_consumed_ratio=item.recent_average_consumed_ratio,
   100	        sample_count=item.sample_count,
   101	        reason=item.reason,
   102	    )
   103	
   104	
   105	def to_device_scan_response(card, meal, guidance_items) -> DeviceRfidScanResponse:
   106	    return DeviceRfidScanResponse(
   107	        user=DeviceUserResponse(
   108	            user_id=card.user.id,
   109	            login_id=card.user.login_id,
   110	            name=card.user.name,
   111	            student_number=card.user.student_number,
   112	        ),
   113	        meal=DeviceMealResponse(**to_meal_response(meal).model_dump()),
   114	        menu_guidance=guidance_items,
   115	    )
   116	
   117	
   118	def to_admin_dashboard_response(data: dict) -> AdminDashboardResponse:
   119	    return AdminDashboardResponse(**data)
   120	
   121	
   122	def to_leftover_summary_items(items: list[dict]) -> list[LeftoverSummaryItemResponse]:
   123	    return [LeftoverSummaryItemResponse(**item) for item in items]

===== FILE: app/api/v1/endpoints/meal_records.py =====
     1	from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends
     2	
     3	from app.api.mappers.response_mappers import to_meal_record_response
     4	from app.api.dependencies import get_meal_record_service, get_nutrition_service
     5	from app.core.security import get_current_user, require_admin
     6	from app.schemas.common import CommonResponse
     7	from app.schemas.meal_record import MealRecordDetailResponse
     8	from app.services.meal_record_service import MealRecordService
     9	from app.services.nutrition_service import NutritionService
    10	
    11	router = APIRouter(tags=["Meal Records"])
    12	
    13	
    14	@router.get("/me/meal-records/{meal_record_id}", response_model=CommonResponse[MealRecordDetailResponse])
    15	def get_my_record(
    16	    meal_record_id: int,
    17	    current_user=Depends(get_current_user),
    18	    service: MealRecordService = Depends(get_meal_record_service),
    19	    nutrition_service: NutritionService = Depends(get_nutrition_service),
    20	):
    21	    record = service.assert_owner(meal_record_id, current_user.id)
    22	    return CommonResponse(message="식사 기록 상세입니다.", data=to_meal_record_response(record, nutrition_service))
    23	
    24	
    25	@router.get("/admin/meal-records", response_model=CommonResponse[list[MealRecordDetailResponse]])
    26	def list_all_records(
    27	    _: object = Depends(require_admin),
    28	    service: MealRecordService = Depends(get_meal_record_service),
    29	    nutrition_service: NutritionService = Depends(get_nutrition_service),
    30	):
    31	    items = service.list_all()
    32	    return CommonResponse(message="전체 식사 기록 목록입니다.", data=[to_meal_record_response(item, nutrition_service) for item in items])

===== FILE: app/api/v1/endpoints/device.py =====
     1	from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, status
     2	
     3	from app.api.dependencies import get_meal_record_service, get_meal_service, get_recommendation_service, get_rfid_service
     4	from app.api.mappers.response_mappers import to_device_scan_response, to_meal_record_response
     5	from app.core.security import require_device_key
     6	from app.schemas.common import CommonResponse
     7	from app.schemas.meal_record import MealRecordDetailResponse
     8	from app.schemas.rfid import DeviceMealRecordCreateRequest, DeviceRfidScanRequest, DeviceRfidScanResponse
     9	from app.services.meal_record_service import MealRecordService
    10	from app.services.meal_service import MealService
    11	from app.services.nutrition_service import NutritionService
    12	from app.services.recommendation_service import RecommendationService
    13	from app.services.rfid_service import RfidService
    14	
    15	router = APIRouter(prefix="/device", tags=["Device"], dependencies=[Depends(require_device_key)])
    16	
    17	
    18	@router.post("/rfid/scan", response_model=CommonResponse[DeviceRfidScanResponse])
    19	def scan_rfid(
    20	    request: DeviceRfidScanRequest,
    21	    rfid_service: RfidService = Depends(get_rfid_service),
    22	    meal_service: MealService = Depends(get_meal_service),
    23	    recommendation_service: RecommendationService = Depends(get_recommendation_service),
    24	):
    25	    card = rfid_service.get_scan_ready_card_by_uid(request.uid)
    26	    meal = meal_service.get_today_meal_by_type(request.meal_type)
    27	    guidance = []
    28	    recommendations = recommendation_service.generate_for_meal(user_id=card.user_id, meal_id=meal.id)
    29	    recommendation_map = {item.meal_menu_item_id: item for item in recommendations}
    30	    user_allergen_codes = {item.allergen.code for item in card.user.allergies}
    31	    for meal_menu_item in meal.meal_menu_items:
    32	        menu_allergen_codes = {link.allergen.code for link in meal_menu_item.menu.allergens}
    33	        matched = sorted(user_allergen_codes & menu_allergen_codes)
    34	        rec = recommendation_map[meal_menu_item.id]
    35	        guidance.append(
    36	            {
    37	                "meal_menu_item_id": meal_menu_item.id,
    38	                "menu_id": meal_menu_item.menu_id,
    39	                "menu_name": meal_menu_item.menu.name,
    40	                "allergens": sorted(menu_allergen_codes),
    41	                "matched_allergens": matched,
    42	                "is_restricted": bool(matched),
    43	                "recommendation_level": rec.recommendation_level.value,
    44	                "recommended_serving_g": rec.recommended_serving_g,
    45	            }
    46	        )
    47	    return CommonResponse(message="RFID 스캔이 완료되었습니다.", data=to_device_scan_response(card, meal, guidance))
    48	
    49	
    50	@router.post("/meal-records", response_model=CommonResponse[MealRecordDetailResponse], status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)
    51	def create_meal_record(
    52	    request: DeviceMealRecordCreateRequest,
    53	    service: MealRecordService = Depends(get_meal_record_service),
    54	):
    55	    record = service.create_from_rfid(rfid_uid=request.rfid_uid, meal_id=request.meal_id)
    56	    return CommonResponse(message="식사 기록이 생성되었습니다.", data=to_meal_record_response(record, NutritionService()))

===== FILE: app/api/v1/endpoints/meal_images.py =====
     1	from io import BytesIO
     2	
     3	from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, File, UploadFile, status
     4	from fastapi.responses import FileResponse, StreamingResponse
     5	
     6	from app.api.dependencies import get_image_service, get_meal_record_service
     7	from app.api.mappers.response_mappers import to_meal_image_response
     8	from app.core.security import get_current_user
     9	from app.schemas.common import CommonResponse
    10	from app.schemas.meal_image import MealImageResponse, MealImageUploadResponse
    11	from app.services.image_service import ImageService
    12	from app.services.meal_record_service import MealRecordService
    13	from app.utils.enums import ImageType
    14	
    15	router = APIRouter(tags=["Meal Images"])
    16	
    17	
    18	@router.post("/me/meal-records/{meal_record_id}/images/before", response_model=CommonResponse[MealImageUploadResponse], status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)
    19	def upload_my_before_image(
    20	    meal_record_id: int,
    21	    file: UploadFile = File(...),
    22	    current_user=Depends(get_current_user),
    23	    image_service: ImageService = Depends(get_image_service),
    24	    record_service: MealRecordService = Depends(get_meal_record_service),
    25	):
    26	    record_service.assert_owner(meal_record_id, current_user.id)
    27	    image = image_service.upload_image(meal_record_id, ImageType.BEFORE, file)
    28	    return CommonResponse(message="식전 이미지가 업로드되었습니다.", data=MealImageUploadResponse(image_id=image.id, image_url=f"/api/v1/me/meal-images/{image.id}"))
    29	
    30	
    31	@router.post("/me/meal-records/{meal_record_id}/images/after", response_model=CommonResponse[MealImageUploadResponse], status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)
    32	def upload_my_after_image(
    33	    meal_record_id: int,
    34	    file: UploadFile = File(...),
    35	    current_user=Depends(get_current_user),
    36	    image_service: ImageService = Depends(get_image_service),
    37	    record_service: MealRecordService = Depends(get_meal_record_service),
    38	):
    39	    record_service.assert_owner(meal_record_id, current_user.id)
    40	    image = image_service.upload_image(meal_record_id, ImageType.AFTER, file)
    41	    return CommonResponse(message="식후 이미지가 업로드되었습니다.", data=MealImageUploadResponse(image_id=image.id, image_url=f"/api/v1/me/meal-images/{image.id}"))
    42	
    43	
    44	@router.get("/me/meal-records/{meal_record_id}/images", response_model=CommonResponse[list[MealImageResponse]])
    45	def list_my_images(
    46	    meal_record_id: int,
    47	    current_user=Depends(get_current_user),
    48	    image_service: ImageService = Depends(get_image_service),
    49	    record_service: MealRecordService = Depends(get_meal_record_service),
    50	):
    51	    record_service.assert_owner(meal_record_id, current_user.id)
    52	    images = image_service.list_images(meal_record_id)
    53	    return CommonResponse(message="이미지 목록입니다.", data=[to_meal_image_response(image) for image in images])
    54	
    55	
    56	@router.get("/me/meal-images/{image_id}")
    57	def get_my_meal_image(image_id: int, current_user=Depends(get_current_user), image_service: ImageService = Depends(get_image_service)):
    58	    image = image_service.get_image_for_user(image_id, current_user.id, is_admin=(getattr(current_user.role, "value", current_user.role) == "ADMIN"))
    59	    headers = {"X-Content-Type-Options": "nosniff"}
    60	    path = image_service.resolve_image_path(image)
    61	    if path is not None:
    62	        return FileResponse(path=path, media_type=image.mime_type, headers=headers)
    63	    return StreamingResponse(BytesIO(image_service.read_image_bytes(image)), media_type=image.mime_type, headers=headers)

     1	from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, Query, status
     2	
     3	from app.api.dependencies import get_menu_service
     4	from app.core.security import require_admin
     5	from app.schemas.common import CommonResponse
     6	from app.schemas.menu import MenuCreateRequest, MenuListResponse, MenuResponse, MenuUpdateRequest
     7	from app.services.menu_service import MenuService
     8	
     9	router = APIRouter(tags=["Menus"])
    10	
    11	
    12	def _menu_response(menu) -> MenuResponse:
    13	    return MenuResponse(
    14	        id=menu.id,
    15	        name=menu.name,
    16	        standard_serving_g=menu.standard_serving_g,
    17	        calories_per_100g=menu.calories_per_100g,
    18	        carbohydrate_per_100g=menu.carbohydrate_per_100g,
    19	        protein_per_100g=menu.protein_per_100g,
    20	        fat_per_100g=menu.fat_per_100g,
    21	        is_active=menu.is_active,
    22	        created_at=menu.created_at,
    23	        updated_at=menu.updated_at,
    24	        ingredients=[link.ingredient.name for link in menu.ingredients],
    25	        allergen_codes=[link.allergen.code for link in menu.allergens],
    26	    )
    27	
    28	
    29	@router.post("/admin/menus", response_model=CommonResponse[MenuResponse], status_code=status.HTTP_201_CREATED)
    30	def create_menu(request: MenuCreateRequest, _: object = Depends(require_admin), service: MenuService = Depends(get_menu_service)):
    31	    return CommonResponse(message="메뉴가 등록되었습니다.", data=_menu_response(service.create_menu(request)))
    32	
    33	
    34	@router.get("/menus", response_model=CommonResponse[MenuListResponse])
    35	def list_menus(include_inactive: bool = Query(default=False), service: MenuService = Depends(get_menu_service)):
    36	    items = service.list_menus(include_inactive=include_inactive)
    37	    return CommonResponse(message="메뉴 목록입니다.", data=MenuListResponse(items=[_menu_response(item) for item in items], total=len(items)))
    38	
    39	
    40	@router.get("/menus/{menu_id}", response_model=CommonResponse[MenuResponse])
    41	def get_menu(menu_id: int, service: MenuService = Depends(get_menu_service)):
    42	    return CommonResponse(message="메뉴 상세입니다.", data=_menu_response(service.get_menu(menu_id)))
    43	
    44	
    45	@router.patch("/admin/menus/{menu_id}", response_model=CommonResponse[MenuResponse])
    46	def update_menu(menu_id: int, request: MenuUpdateRequest, _: object = Depends(require_admin), service: MenuService = Depends(get_menu_service)):
    47	    return CommonResponse(message="메뉴가 수정되었습니다.", data=_menu_response(service.update_menu(menu_id, request)))
